Sherry narrows her eyes, her tone turning playful but insistent.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re being suspicious.  

  

Jeff smirks, leaning back against the couch.  

  

**JEFF**  

Am I?  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yes, you are. And now I really want to know.  

  

Jeff shakes his head, clearly enjoying the game.  

  

**JEFF**  

Sorry. Not happening.  

  

Sherry sits up straighter, her expression mischievous.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Oh, I’ll get it out of you.  

  

Jeff chuckles, crossing his arms.  

  

**JEFF**  

Good luck with that.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Feminine Charms**  

  

Sherry shifts closer to Jeff, her voice dropping to a sultry tone.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You know, I have my ways.  

  

Jeff raises an eyebrow, clearly intrigued but skeptical.  

  

**JEFF**  

Oh, yeah?  

  

Sherry leans in, her hand lightly tracing along his arm.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I can be very persuasive.  

  

Jeff smirks, his tone teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

I’m sure you can.  

  

Sherry moves even closer, her lips brushing against his ear as she whispers.  

  

**SHERRY**  

So, who’s the mystery texter?  

  

Jeff laughs, pulling back slightly.  

  

**JEFF**  

Nice try. But you’re not getting it out of me.  

  

Sherry pouts, though her smile betrays her amusement.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re no fun.  

  

**JEFF**  

(smiling)  

And yet, here you are.  

  

---

  

**Tension and Trust**  

  

Sherry sits back, crossing her arms as she studies him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You know, keeping secrets isn’t exactly the best way to build trust.  

  

Jeff’s smile fades slightly, his tone softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

It’s not a secret. It’s just… personal.  

  

Sherry’s expression shifts, her tone more understanding.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay. I can respect that.  

  

Jeff leans forward, his voice quieter now.  

  

**JEFF**  

Thanks.  

  

Sherry smiles faintly, her voice light again.  

  

**SHERRY**  

But if it turns out you’re planning something weird, I’m holding this over your head.  

  

Jeff laughs, reaching for another cookie.  

  

**JEFF**  

Fair enough.  

  

---

  

**Building Connection**  

  

The mood lightens again as Sherry leans into Jeff, resting her head on his shoulder.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re lucky I like you.  

  

Jeff grins, his tone teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

I know.  

  

They sit in comfortable silence for a moment, the camera lingering on their easy closeness.  

  

---

### **Scene 30: Sherry’s Late-Night Curiosity**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s bedroom, late at night. The room is dimly lit by the faint glow of a bedside lamp. Jeff is sound asleep after their passionate evening, leaving Sherry alone with her thoughts and a persistent curiosity about the earlier text messages. Her attempt to uncover Jeff’s secrets only deepens her intrigue, setting the stage for meaningful and playful interactions in the coming day.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S BEDROOM – NIGHT**  

  

The camera pans across the room, focusing on Jeff sprawled out on the bed, his breathing steady and deep. Sherry lies beside him, her head propped on one hand as she watches him sleep.  

  

Her expression is soft but tinged with curiosity, the earlier mystery of Jeff’s text messages lingering in her mind.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

You could’ve just let it go. But no, you had to be all mysterious about it.  

  

She glances at Jeff’s phone on the nightstand, the screen dark. Her gaze flickers back to him, ensuring he’s still asleep.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Just one little peek. It’s not like I’m stealing state secrets.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Attempt to Peek**  

  

Sherry carefully reaches over Jeff, grabbing the phone from the nightstand. The faint buzz of the screen lighting up seems louder than it should, and she freezes, glancing at him.  

  

Jeff shifts slightly but doesn’t wake.  

  

Sherry relaxes, tilting the phone toward her. The lock screen displays the last message:  

  

**ON SCREEN**: “JOE ELLIOT: U got it. It will ship tonite!”  

  

Sherry frowns, whispering to herself.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Joe Elliot?  

  

Her brow furrows deeper as she processes the name.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

The *Joe Elliot*? Of Def Leppard?  

  

She tries to unlock the phone, but it requires a passcode. Sighing, she places it back on the nightstand.  

  

---

  

**Contemplating Jeff’s Mystery**  

  

Sherry lies back on the bed, staring at the ceiling. Her mind races, alternating between confusion and amusement.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Okay, so maybe you weren’t texting another woman. But what the hell is this about shipping?  

  

She smirks, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Typical Jeff. Always full of surprises.  

  

Her gaze shifts back to him, her smile softening as she watches him sleep.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

You’re impossible, rock star. But maybe I like it that way.  

  

---

  

**Foreshadowing Playful Interactions**  

  

The camera fades into the next morning, mirroring the earlier playful energy of their day. Sherry sits at the kitchen table, sipping coffee, her expression thoughtful as she devises ways to tease Jeff about the text without revealing her late-night snooping.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

So, you want to keep secrets? Fine. Let’s see how you like being on the other side.  

  

Her smirk grows as she takes another sip.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Let the games begin.  

  

---

  

**Setting the Tone for the Day**  

  

Sherry glances out the window at the rising sun, her expression a mix of mischief and affection.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe today’s about balance. A little meaningful connection, a little playful revenge.  

  

The sound of Jeff stirring in the bedroom draws her attention. She grins, setting her coffee down.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Let’s see what you’ve got, rock star.  

  

The camera lingers on her amused expression before fading out.  

  

---

### **Scene 31: Morning Teasing and Navigating Curiosity**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s bedroom, transitioning to the kitchen. The warm morning light filters through the curtains as Jeff wakes up, his groggy desire for intimacy clashing with Sherry’s playful teasing about the mystery text messages. Jeff tries to sidestep her curiosity without spoiling the surprise he’s orchestrated.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S BEDROOM – MORNING**  

  

The soft light of dawn streams into the room. Sherry sits on the edge of the bed, pulling on a pair of cozy socks, her hair slightly tousled. Jeff stirs under the covers, groaning softly as he rolls onto his side.  

  

**JEFF**  

(murmuring)  

Morning.  

  

Sherry glances back, smirking.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Morning, rock star.  

  

Jeff stretches lazily, reaching out to her.  

  

**JEFF**  

Come back to bed.  

  

Sherry laughs, standing up and crossing her arms.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Oh, so now you’re feeling affectionate?  

  

Jeff props himself up on one elbow, grinning.  

  

**JEFF**  

Can you blame me?  

  

Sherry raises an eyebrow, her tone turning teasing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Maybe. Or maybe I’m still trying to figure out who you were texting last night.  

  

Jeff freezes for a moment, his grin faltering.  

  

**JEFF**  

(playing dumb)  

Texting?  

  

Sherry nods, stepping closer to the bed and leaning down, her expression mischievous.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. You know, all those messages you sent while we were on the couch? The ones you wouldn’t tell me about?  

  

Jeff chuckles nervously, rubbing the back of his neck.  

  

**JEFF**  

Oh, that.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Uh-huh. That.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Playful Teasing**  

  

Sherry sits on the edge of the bed, her tone light but persistent.  

  

**SHERRY**  

So, are you going to tell me who it was?  

  

Jeff shakes his head, his grin returning.  

  

**JEFF**  

Nope.  

  

Sherry leans closer, her voice dropping to a sultry tone.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Come on, Jeff. You can tell me.  

  

Jeff laughs, sitting up and gently pushing her back playfully.  

  

**JEFF**  

Nice try. But I’m not ruining the surprise.  

  

Sherry narrows her eyes, her tone mock suspicious.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Surprise, huh? And here I thought you were texting Joe Elliot.  

  

Jeff’s eyes widen briefly before he recovers, smirking.  

  

**JEFF**  

What makes you think that?  

  

Sherry grins, standing up and crossing her arms.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Oh, just a hunch.  

  

Jeff swings his legs over the side of the bed, standing and stretching.  

  

**JEFF**  

Well, whatever you think, you’re just going to have to wait.  

  

---

  

**INT. KITCHEN – MORNING**  

  

Jeff leans against the counter, sipping coffee as Sherry moves around the kitchen, pretending to be disinterested.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(half-muttering)  

A surprise, huh? You’re lucky I’m patient.  

  

Jeff chuckles, setting his mug down.  

  

**JEFF**  

It’ll be worth it.  

  

Sherry glances at him, her tone playful but curious.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Fine. But if this surprise turns out to be something weird, I’m never letting you live it down.  

  

Jeff smirks, his voice warm.  

  

**JEFF**  

Deal.  

  

Sherry laughs, stepping closer to him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You know, you’re pretty lucky I like you.  

  

Jeff wraps an arm around her waist, pulling her closer.  

  

**JEFF**  

I’m starting to think I am.  

  

---

  

**Building Anticipation**  

  

Sherry rests her hands on his chest, her tone softening slightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re really not going to give me a hint?  

  

Jeff shakes his head, his grin mischievous.  

  

**JEFF**  

Not a chance.  

  

Sherry sighs dramatically, though her smile lingers.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Fine. But if you’re keeping secrets, don’t be surprised if I do the same.  

  

Jeff laughs, leaning down to kiss her forehead.  

  

**JEFF**  

Fair enough.  

  

---

  

**Foreshadowing the Surprise**  

  

As they settle into the morning routine, the camera lingers on Jeff’s expression as he watches Sherry. His gaze softens, a flicker of nervous excitement breaking through his usual calm demeanor.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

She’s going to love it.  

  

The scene fades as Sherry teases him one last time, the playful tension between them keeping the audience invested in their deepening connection.  

  

---

  

**CAMERA SHOTS AND SOUND EDITING**  

  

**Camera Shots**:  

- Close-ups of Sherry’s playful expressions and Jeff’s nervous but affectionate reactions.  

- Medium shots of their physical closeness, highlighting their growing intimacy.  

- A wide shot of the cozy kitchen, framed by the morning light.  

  

**Sound Editing**:  

- The soft clink of mugs and the hum of the coffee maker add realism to the scene.  

- A light, playful score underscores their teasing banter, fading into a softer melody during tender moments.  

  

---

### **Scene 32: Anticipation Builds**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s house in the morning, transitioning to her workday at the university’s Senior Accountant office. Sherry’s curiosity about Jeff’s surprise grows throughout the day, creating a humorous, buzzing atmosphere in her office. The eventual arrival of the FedEx delivery woman with an enormous package sends the office into a frenzy.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S BATHROOM – MORNING**  

  

Steam fills the air as water cascades from the showerhead. Jeff stands under the stream, his hair damp and disheveled, as Sherry steps in beside him, her expression both playful and hurried.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(grinning)  

All right, rock star. Make it quick. I’ve got a nine-to-five to get to.  

  

Jeff smirks, pulling her closer under the water.  

  

**JEFF**  

Quick? You’re ruining my process.  

  

Sherry rolls her eyes, laughing softly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’ve got five minutes, maybe ten if you’re charming.  

  

Jeff leans down, his voice low and teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

Oh, I’m always charming.  

  

Sherry chuckles, shaking her head as she lathers soap onto her arms.  

  

**SHERRY**  

We’ll see about that.  

  

The camera lingers on their playful interaction, capturing their shared intimacy before fading to the next scene.  

  

---

  

**INT. UNIVERSITY CAMPUS OFFICE – MORNING**  

  

The bustling energy of the office contrasts with Sherry’s focused demeanor as she sits at her desk, typing on her computer. A framed photo of her kids and a mug reading “World’s Okayest Mom” sit beside neatly stacked folders.  

  

Her mind drifts as she glances at her phone, the curiosity from earlier gnawing at her.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s up to something. And it’s probably ridiculous.  

  

A coworker, JANE, pokes her head into Sherry’s office, her tone cheerful.  

  

**JANE**  

You’ve been smiling all morning. Got a secret admirer?  

  

Sherry laughs, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Not a secret, exactly. But there might be something… interesting on the way.  

  

Jane raises an eyebrow, intrigued.  

  

**JANE**  

Ooh, do tell.  

  

Sherry grins, leaning back in her chair.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Let’s just say I’m expecting a surprise.  

  

---

  

**Office Buzz and Fake Outs**  

  

Throughout the day, Sherry’s anticipation grows, drawing the attention of her coworkers.  

  

**MONTAGE**:  

  

1. **Mid-Morning**: Sherry checks her phone repeatedly, biting her lip as she refreshes her email for shipping updates.  

2. **Lunch Hour**: A delivery person walks past the office with a box, and Sherry leans forward eagerly, only to slump back when they head to another department.  

3. **Afternoon Meeting**: During a Zoom call, Sherry’s eyes dart toward the window every time she hears footsteps outside. Her coworkers exchange amused glances.  

  

---

  

**INT. UNIVERSITY CAMPUS OFFICE – 3 PM**  

  

The sound of laughter and casual conversation fills the air as Sherry organizes her desk. Suddenly, a commotion breaks out near the entrance.  

  

**JANE (O.S.)**  

Oh my God, Sherry! You’ve got a delivery!  

  

Sherry stands, peering out of her office just as a FedEx delivery woman enters, struggling with a gigantic package. The box is almost comically large, dwarfing the driver.  

  

The entire office falls silent, everyone staring as the driver sets the package down with a huff.  

  

**FEDEX DRIVER**  

Delivery for Sherry Sims-Greene.  

  

Sherry blinks, her eyes widening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s… for me?  

  

The driver grins, handing her a clipboard.  

  

**FEDEX DRIVER**  

Sure is. Sign here.  

  

Sherry quickly signs, her coworkers gathering around with excited whispers.  

  

**COWORKER 1**  

What’s in it?  

  

**COWORKER 2**  

Looks like a fridge!  

  

**JANE**  

Sherry, is this from your mystery admirer?  

  

Sherry smiles nervously, her curiosity reaching its peak.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I guess we’re about to find out.  

  

---

  

**Opening the Package**  

  

With the help of Jane and a few others, Sherry carefully peels away the packaging. The crowd gasps as she reveals an enormous, beautifully framed photo of Def Leppard, each band member’s autograph scrawled in bold silver marker across the glossy surface.  

  

In the corner, a handwritten note reads:  

  

**“To Sherry, the sweetest fan we’ve never met. Thanks for making one of our guys smile. Rock on! – Joe Elliot and the band”**  

  

Sherry stares at the gift, her jaw dropping as her coworkers erupt in excited chatter.  

  

**JANE**  

Sherry! This is incredible!  

  

**COWORKER 1**  

Who sent it?  

  

Sherry laughs, her cheeks flushing as she gently touches the frame.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I have a pretty good idea.  

  

Her coworkers cheer, patting her on the back as the camera lingers on her beaming expression.  

  

---

  

**CAMERA SHOTS AND SOUND EDITING**  

  

**Camera Shots**:  

- Medium shots of Sherry’s growing anticipation at her desk, capturing her playful expressions and the reactions of her coworkers.  

- A close-up of the massive package as the FedEx driver delivers it, emphasizing its size and the resulting commotion.  

- A wide shot of the office crowding around Sherry as she opens the gift, framing the excitement and laughter.  

  

**Sound Editing**:  

- The hum of office chatter and the sound of footsteps build the anticipation throughout the day.  

- A triumphant musical swell underscores the reveal of the gift, fading into the laughter and cheers of Sherry’s coworkers.  

  

---

### **Scene 33: Sherry’s Reaction and Plans**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s house, early evening. Sherry returns home after an eventful day at work with the massive framed photo of Def Leppard, overwhelmed by Jeff’s extravagant gesture. Her emotions run the gamut as she processes his thoughtfulness and her feelings for him. Alone in the quiet of her home, she decides to thank Jeff in a way that matches his intensity while grappling with her swirling emotions.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – EVENING**  

  

Sherry struggles through the front door, balancing her purse and the enormous framed photo. She sets it down carefully against the wall, stepping back to take it in.  

  

The glossy surface reflects the soft glow of the living room lamp. The autographs and handwritten note gleam under the light. Sherry stares at it, her hands on her hips, a mix of emotions playing across her face.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Okay. Overkill? Definitely.  

  

She tilts her head, her expression softening.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But thoughtful? Sweet? Unbelievably romantic? Yeah. That too.  

  

Sherry sinks onto the couch, staring at the photo as she runs a hand through her hair.  

  

---

  

**Kaleidoscope of Emotions**  

  

**JOYFULNESS**  

Sherry grins suddenly, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

I mean, who else gets something like this? A personal gift from Joe Elliot, signed and framed like it came straight out of a museum.  

  

She laughs softly, hugging a throw pillow to her chest.  

  

**GRATITUDE**  

Her smile fades into a look of quiet wonder.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He didn’t have to do this. He went out of his way, just to make me smile.  

  

Her eyes glisten as she exhales deeply, the gratitude settling in her chest.  

  

**BEWILDERMENT**  

Her brows furrow, and she leans forward, staring at the photo again.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But seriously… a near life-sized photo? For my office? Does he think I’m going to hang this up next to the copier?  

  

She bites her lip, a half-smile tugging at the corners of her mouth.  

  

**RANDINESS**  

Her gaze softens, and her cheeks flush as she remembers the morning.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

And he still had the nerve to leave me breathless before flying off to New York like it was nothing.  

  

She leans back against the couch, fanning herself with one hand.  

  

**HOPEFULNESS**  

Her expression turns more serious as she looks at the photo again.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe this isn’t just about the gift. Maybe it’s about what kind of man he is. Thoughtful. Generous.  

  

A faint smile returns as she crosses her arms.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe this could be something real.  

  

**SELF-DOUBT**  

The smile falters, and her shoulders tense.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Or maybe it’s too much. What if I can’t keep up with him? His world, his pace?  

  

She shakes her head quickly, standing up and brushing off the thought.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Decisions**  

  

Sherry walks to the framed photo, running her fingers lightly along the edge. Her reflection stares back at her in the glossy surface, and she smiles faintly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

No. I’m not letting doubt win tonight.  

  

She grabs her phone from the coffee table and dials Jeff. The phone rings a few times before he picks up.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

(cheerfully)  

Hey, Sherry. Did it arrive?  

  

Sherry’s grin widens, her voice a mix of laughter and warmth.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Did it arrive? Jeff, it’s the size of a small car!  

  

Jeff laughs on the other end of the line.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

Too much?  

  

**SHERRY**  

Way too much. But also… perfect. Thank you.  

  

Jeff’s voice softens, his tone sincere.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

I’m glad you liked it.  

  

Sherry sits back on the couch, her smile turning mischievous.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Liked it? Rock star, you’ve set the bar so high, I don’t think anyone else could ever top this.  

  

Jeff chuckles, the sound warm and easy.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

Good. That was the idea.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Next Steps**  

  

After the call ends, Sherry sits in thoughtful silence for a moment. She suddenly stands, her expression resolute.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

If he’s willing to go out of his way to make me feel special, I can do the same.  

  

She heads to her desk, pulling out stationery and a pen. The camera lingers on her as she begins to write a heartfelt note, her expression softening with each word.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Step one: write something that’ll make him smile. Step two… well, we’ll see about step two.  

  

The scene ends with a close-up of Sherry’s hand as she writes the opening lines of the note:  

  

**INSERT HANDWRITTEN NOTE**:  

"Dear Jeff, I don’t even know where to begin, but here’s a start: you’re something else…"  

  

---

### **Scene 34: The Challenge**  

**Setting**: Parallel narratives between Sherry’s growing anxiety at home and Jeff’s professional obligations in New York City. The misalignment of their communication escalates into a pivotal moment that challenges their connection, highlighting the fragility of their budding relationship.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – DAY**  

  

Sherry sits on her couch, wearing only her Def Leppard t-shirt, her phone in hand. She angles the camera for a playful selfie, snapping a photo with a flirtatious smile. After a moment of consideration, she sends it to Jeff with a winking emoji:  

  

**TEXT**: *“Missing you, rock star. 😉”*  

  

Sherry sets the phone down, waiting for the familiar buzz of his near-instant response. Seconds turn into minutes. She picks up the phone again, frowning at the lack of notification.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Weird. He’s usually faster than this.  

  

She snaps another selfie, this time pouting, and sends it.  

  

**TEXT**: *“Hello? You out there? 😘”*  

  

Still nothing. Sherry’s brow furrows, her mind racing.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Doesn’t he think I’m… enough?  

  

---

  

**INT. WABC TV STUDIO – DAY**  

  

Jeff sits under bright lights on a television set, mid-interview with a *WABC* host. The backdrop behind them features vibrant images of the band Commuted and the title: *“A Rock Revival: Commuted’s Next Chapter.”*  

  

The host leans forward, smiling.  

  

**HOST**  

So, Jeff, this new album, *English Major and Sea Shanties,* has quite the title. Where did the inspiration come from?  

  

Jeff chuckles, leaning back in his chair.  

  

**JEFF**  

Well, Gilley came up with it, and it stuck. It’s a mix of humor and nostalgia for the weird, eclectic stories we’ve collected over the years.  

  

The host nods, laughing along.  

  

**HOST**  

And fans are already buzzing. Are you ready for the tour life again?  

  

Jeff grins, though it falters slightly.  

  

**JEFF**  

Let’s just say I’m taking it one step at a time.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – CONTINUOUS**  

  

Sherry’s frustration mounts as she takes another selfie, this time removing the t-shirt and holding it against her chest. She types a new message:  

  

**TEXT**: *“You’ve gone silent on me, rock star. What gives?”*  

  

She hesitates for a moment before hitting send.  

  

The lack of response feels like a slap. Her frustration boils over, and she begins snapping photo after photo, sending them in rapid succession. Each image grows increasingly less playful and more desperate, her expression shifting to anger and sadness.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

How can he just… ignore me?  

  

Her final photo captures her tear-streaked face as she collapses onto the couch, phone clutched tightly in her hand.  

  

---

  

**INT. WABC GREEN ROOM – LATER**  

  

Jeff enters the green room after the interview, running a hand through his hair. He sets down his guitar case and phone charger, reaching for his phone.  

  

The screen lights up with 183 missed messages, the notification sound chiming incessantly as more messages arrive. Jeff raises an eyebrow, unlocking the phone.  

  

**INSERT PHONE SCREEN**: The first few photos are playful selfies of Sherry in her Def Leppard t-shirt, accompanied by flirty messages.  

  

Jeff’s smile softens as he scrolls through, murmuring to himself.  

  

**JEFF**  

She’s something else.  

  

As the photos grow darker, Jeff’s smile fades. His jaw tightens, his expression turning grim. He stops scrolling, staring at an image of Sherry’s tearful face.  

  

The phone chimes one last time, signaling the final photo. Jeff exhales sharply, rubbing his temples.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

What the hell happened?  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – NIGHT**  

  

Sherry sits curled up on the couch, her phone lying discarded beside her. Her face is blotchy from crying, her eyes red and puffy. She picks up the phone again, hesitating before dialing her sister.  

  

**SPLIT-SCREEN**: **SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM** / **HER SISTER’S KITCHEN**  

  

Her sister answers on the second ring, her tone light.  

  

**SISTER**  

Sherry? What’s going on?  

  

Sherry takes a shaky breath, her voice cracking.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I messed up. I messed up so bad.  

  

Her sister’s tone shifts to concern.  

  

**SISTER**  

What happened?  

  

Sherry launches into a tearful confession, recounting everything from the weekend with Jeff to the photos she sent that day.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I thought it was fun. I thought he’d laugh, or flirt back, but… nothing. Not a single word.  

  

Her sister sighs, her tone soothing but firm.  

  

**SISTER**  

Sherry, you’ve got to remember who you’re dealing with. He’s a rock star. He’s used to living at a different pace.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(whispering)  

So, what does that mean for me?  

  

Her sister pauses, her voice softening.  

  

**SISTER**  

It means you need to talk to him. Not through photos, not through games. Just… talk.  

  

Sherry nods slowly, wiping her eyes.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay.  

  

---

### **Scene 35: Jeff’s Response**  

**Setting**: The green room at WABC in New York City. Jeff is reeling from Sherry’s flood of messages, torn between his initial appreciation for her boldness and concern over her evident emotional spiral. He decides to respond thoughtfully, despite his own discomfort and sensory overload.  

  

---

  

**INT. WABC GREEN ROOM – NIGHT**  

  

Jeff sits on the couch, his phone in hand. The room is quiet except for the faint hum of studio equipment in the distance. His thumb hovers over the screen as he scrolls back through Sherry’s photos, his expression a mix of admiration and unease.  

  

**INSERT PHONE SCREEN**: A playful selfie of Sherry wearing only her Def Leppard t-shirt, smiling coyly.  

  

Jeff pauses on the image, his lips twitching into a small smile.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

She’s bold. I’ll give her that.  

  

He swipes forward, his smile fading as the photos grow darker in tone. The accompanying messages flash across the screen:  

  

**TEXTS**:  

- *“Don’t you like me?”*  

- *“Am I not good enough?”*  

- *“What am I even doing here?”*  

  

Jeff rubs his temple, exhaling sharply.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

This… is a lot.  

  

He closes his eyes for a moment, grounding himself. When he opens them again, his gaze lands on the playful selfie from earlier.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

Okay. Start with something simple.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Bold Decision**  

  

Jeff taps the screen, setting Sherry’s playful photo as his lock screen image. He stares at the phone for a moment, a faint smirk crossing his face.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

Probably not the smartest move. But she *is* kind of hot.  

  

He sets the phone down and leans back against the couch, his expression growing more thoughtful.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

Now, how do I handle… everything else?  

  

Jeff picks up the phone again, swiping to Sherry’s contact and hitting the call button.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – NIGHT**  

  

Sherry sits on the couch, clutching her phone tightly. Her sister’s voice echoes faintly from the other end of a call.  

  

**SISTER (V.O.)**  

You still there?  

  

Sherry blinks, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. Sorry.  

  

Her phone vibrates in her hand, and she glances down to see Jeff’s name flashing on the screen.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(softly)  

It’s him.  

  

**SISTER (V.O.)**  

Then hang up with me and talk to him.  

  

Sherry hesitates before ending the call with her sister. She answers Jeff’s call, her voice trembling slightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Hello?  

  

---

  

**The Conversation**  

  

**SPLIT-SCREEN**: **JEFF IN THE GREEN ROOM** / **SHERRY IN HER LIVING ROOM**  

  

Jeff’s tone is calm but tinged with concern.  

  

**JEFF**  

Hey.  

  

Sherry bites her lip, her voice soft.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Hi.  

  

A beat of silence stretches between them before Jeff speaks again.  

  

**JEFF**  

I got your messages.  

  

Sherry closes her eyes, exhaling shakily.  

  

**SHERRY**  

All of them?  

  

**JEFF**  

(softly)  

Yeah.  

  

Sherry winces, her voice barely above a whisper.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I went a little overboard.  

  

Jeff chuckles lightly, though his tone remains gentle.  

  

**JEFF**  

A little?  

  

Sherry laughs softly, though it’s tinged with embarrassment.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay. A lot.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Approach**  

  

Jeff leans forward, resting his elbows on his knees.  

  

**JEFF**  

Look, the first few… they were great. I appreciated them.  

  

Sherry’s cheeks flush, a faint smile tugging at her lips.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You did?  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. You’re beautiful, Sherry. And bold.  

  

Sherry’s smile fades slightly, her voice quieter.  

  

**SHERRY**  

But?  

  

Jeff sighs, running a hand through his hair.  

  

**JEFF**  

But… when it started to feel like something else, like you were upset… that worried me.  

  

Sherry swallows hard, nodding even though he can’t see her.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I just… I thought maybe you didn’t like me.  

  

Jeff’s tone softens further.  

  

**JEFF**  

Sherry, I like you. A lot. But I was in the middle of something, and I couldn’t respond right away. That doesn’t mean I wasn’t thinking about you.  

  

Sherry exhales slowly, her tension easing slightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I guess I got in my own head.  

  

Jeff smiles faintly, his voice lightening.  

  

**JEFF**  

I’ve been there.  

  

---

  

**The Gesture**  

  

Jeff hesitates before speaking again.  

  

**JEFF**  

You know, I liked one of your photos so much, I made it my lock screen.  

  

Sherry’s eyes widen, a mix of shock and amusement crossing her face.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You didn’t.  

  

**JEFF**  

(smiling)  

I did.  

  

Sherry laughs, her voice warming.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Which one?  

  

**JEFF**  

The one where you’re still in the shirt, smiling like you’ve got a secret.  

  

Sherry shakes her head, a genuine laugh escaping her lips.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re unbelievable.  

  

Jeff grins, his voice softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

And you’re amazing.  

  

---

### **Scene 36: Sherry Processes the Conversation**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s living room, late evening. The quiet stillness of the house contrasts with the whirlwind of emotions and thoughts racing through Sherry’s mind. While relieved by her call with Jeff, she begins to rationalize his decision to use her photo and wrestles with her growing insecurities, particularly about Kathy, whom she starts to view as a potential threat.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – NIGHT**  

  

Sherry sits cross-legged on the couch, her phone resting on the cushion beside her. The framed Def Leppard photo leans against the wall, half-wrapped in the remaining packaging. A glass of wine sits untouched on the coffee table.  

  

Sherry leans back, exhaling slowly, her expression conflicted.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Okay. So he liked the picture. A lot. Enough to make it his lock screen.  

  

She frowns, her gaze drifting toward the ceiling.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But it wasn’t just a cute selfie. There was a little more… me in it than I usually show.  

  

Her cheeks flush slightly as she covers her face with her hands.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(softly)  

Oh, God. What was I thinking?  

  

She lowers her hands, staring at her phone.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But it’s just one photo. For one person. For *Jeff.* It’s not like he’s going to share it with anyone.  

  

Her brow furrows as her thoughts spiral.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Right?  

  

---

  

**Rationalizing Jeff’s Choice**  

  

Sherry picks up her wine glass, sipping absentmindedly as she continues to mull over the situation.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

I mean, it’s not like he hasn’t seen me like that before. And it’s private. He’s not parading it around onstage.  

  

She sets the glass down, her expression softening slightly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Besides, isn’t this the same guy who’s always going on about respecting women? The whole band does.  

  

Her gaze shifts to the Def Leppard photo, her thoughts turning darker.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Except for Kathy. Miss Holier-Than-Thou. Preaching about women’s empowerment while posing naked on an album cover.  

  

Sherry scoffs, crossing her arms.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

And Wal-Mart carried that damn thing. Hypocrite.  

  

---

  

**First Hint of Dislike for Kathy**  

  

Sherry’s expression hardens as her thoughts settle on Kathy.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

She’s always acting like she’s so much better than everyone else. So much smarter.  

  

She pauses, her frown deepening.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

And then there’s the way Jeff talks about her. Like she’s some kind of legend.  

  

Her grip tightens on the wine glass.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He *would* respect her. Look up to her. Maybe even…  

  

Her jaw clenches, and she sets the glass down abruptly, spilling a few drops onto the table.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

No. Stop. You’re being ridiculous.  

  

She grabs a napkin, wiping up the wine, but her thoughts refuse to relent.  

  

---

  

**Paranoia Creeps In**  

  

Sherry sits back again, her arms crossed tightly over her chest.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

What if there’s something between them? He’s with me now, but what if…  

  

She shakes her head, laughing bitterly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(softly)  

Listen to yourself. You’re losing it.  

  

She stands, pacing the room as her thoughts race.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

It’s not like he’s texting her. It’s not like she’s the one on his lock screen.  

  

Her steps slow as a new thought strikes her, her expression turning wistful.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But does he talk about me like that? Does he admire me the way he admires her?  

  

She sinks onto the couch again, her energy drained.  

  

---

  

**Resolution and Rationalization**  

  

Sherry picks up her phone, staring at the blank screen.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Okay. Enough. He’s with me. He chose me.  

  

Her lips twitch into a faint smile as she recalls Jeff’s words.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

“You’re amazing.”  

  

She sighs, her tension easing slightly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe he’s not perfect. Maybe he doesn’t always think things through. But he’s trying. And so am I.  

  

Her gaze drifts to the Def Leppard photo, and she laughs softly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Besides, if he wanted someone like Kathy, he wouldn’t have sent me that.  

  

She picks up the wine glass, toasting the photo with a faint smirk.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Here’s to being bold.  

  

---

### **Scene 37: Evidence of Kathy**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s mansion near Fort Ancient, above a snow-covered gorge on the Little Miami River. The breathtaking winter landscape contrasts with Sherry’s growing unease as she discovers a striking pointillist nude portrait of Kathy in Jeff’s home. This moment begins to unravel Sherry’s insecurities and sets the stage for tension surrounding Jeff’s past and his connection to Kathy.  

  

---

  

**EXT. JEFF’S MANSION – DAY**  

  

The camera pans over the serene, snow-blanketed landscape. The Little Miami River winds through the gorge below, its surface glinting faintly under the winter sun. Bare trees cast intricate shadows over the snow, creating a stark yet beautiful scene.  

  

Sherry steps out of Jeff’s car, bundled in her coat, her breath visible in the crisp air. She takes in the surroundings, her expression a mix of awe and anticipation.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

This place. It’s like something out of a painting.  

  

Jeff steps around the car, grabbing their bags from the trunk.  

  

**JEFF**  

(cheerfully)  

Wait till spring. This whole area explodes with color.  

  

Sherry smiles faintly, looking back at him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

It’s already incredible.  

  

Jeff grins, slinging a bag over his shoulder.  

  

**JEFF**  

Come on. Let’s get inside before we freeze.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S MANSION – FOYER – CONTINUOUS**  

  

The interior of Jeff’s home is warm and inviting, with rustic wooden beams and large windows that frame the winter landscape outside. A fire crackles in the massive stone fireplace, casting a golden glow over the room.  

  

Sherry shrugs off her coat, glancing around with wide eyes.  

  

**SHERRY**  

This place is… amazing.  

  

Jeff sets the bags down, his tone casual.  

  

**JEFF**  

It’s home.  

  

He gestures toward the large windows overlooking the gorge.  

  

**JEFF**  

Take a look. The view’s even better from up here.  

  

Sherry smiles, wandering toward the windows.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S MANSION – LIVING ROOM – MOMENTS LATER**  

  

As Sherry moves through the house, her gaze lingers on the details: shelves filled with books, framed photos of the band, and eclectic pieces of art.  

  

Her steps falter when she reaches a large pointillist portrait displayed prominently on one wall. The life-sized image depicts a nude woman reclining gracefully, her expression serene. The intricate dots of color give the piece a dreamlike quality, but the subject is unmistakable.  

  

At the bottom of the frame, a small brass plaque reads:  

  

**“Kathy – 1997”**  

  

Sherry stares at the portrait, her chest tightening.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

It’s her.  

  

Her mind races, piecing together fragments of Jeff’s stories and her own insecurities.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Why would he keep this? Display it like this?  

  

Jeff’s voice breaks through her thoughts.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

Everything okay?  

  

---

  

**The Confrontation**  

  

Sherry turns, her expression carefully neutral.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Who’s the artist?  

  

Jeff walks over, glancing at the portrait with a faint smile.  

  

**JEFF**  

An old friend. He did it back when we were starting out.  

  

Sherry crosses her arms, her tone light but probing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Kathy?  

  

Jeff nods, his tone casual.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. He wanted a subject, and she volunteered.  

  

Sherry raises an eyebrow, her voice laced with faint tension.  

  

**SHERRY**  

And you just… kept it?  

  

Jeff shrugs, his tone growing more thoughtful.  

  

**JEFF**  

It’s part of the band’s history. He gave it to me when he moved out west. Said I was the only one who’d appreciate it.  

  

Sherry nods slowly, her gaze shifting back to the portrait.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I’m sure you do.  

  

---

  

**Internal Turmoil**  

  

Sherry forces a smile, turning away from the portrait as her mind churns.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

It’s ancient history. Just a piece of art.  

  

Her gaze drifts toward Jeff, who is rummaging through one of their bags.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But why her? Why keep *this* after all these years?  

  

Her chest tightens as a wave of paranoia washes over her.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Is she more than just a bandmate?  

  

Jeff glances back at her, grinning.  

  

**JEFF**  

Come on. Let me show you the rest of the place.  

  

Sherry nods, her smile stiff as she follows him.  

  

---


### **Scene 38: Sherry’s Discovery**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s mansion bathroom, late evening. After a passionate and exhausting few hours with Jeff, Sherry excuses herself to freshen up. Her curiosity leads her to snoop through the luxurious bathroom, where she uncovers mundane items, potential hints of Jeff’s past struggles, and a more startling discovery: an old box of nearly empty tampons hidden under the sink.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BATHROOM – NIGHT**  

  

The bathroom is stunning, with polished marble countertops, sleek fixtures, and an enormous glass shower. A chandelier hangs overhead, casting a soft, warm glow. Sherry closes the door behind her, leaning against it for a moment, catching her breath.  

  

She looks around, taking in the opulence.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

This bathroom probably cost more than my whole house.  

  

She steps toward the sink, glancing at herself in the oversized mirror. Her hair is tousled, her skin flushed. She smirks faintly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

You’re a mess, Sherry.  

  

---

  

**Curiosity Takes Over**  

  

Sherry splashes cool water on her face, patting it dry with a fluffy white towel. She hesitates, then opens the vanity mirror cabinet, her curiosity getting the better of her.  

  

Inside, she finds a collection of typical bathroom items: toothpaste, floss, over-the-counter painkillers, and a few prescription bottles. She picks up one of the bottles, turning it over in her hand.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Painkillers. Expired years ago.  

  

She sets it back and notices a small flat mirror and several razor blades tucked in a corner. Her brow furrows.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

For cutting? Or shaving?  

  

Her mind flashes briefly to Jeff’s earlier confessions about his past drug use.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Well, he did say he had a wild phase. At least he’s honest about it.  

  

She closes the cabinet, her gaze drifting toward the sink below. Her curiosity gets the better of her again, and she crouches down to open the cabinet doors.  

  

---

  

**The Unexpected Discovery**  

  

Sherry rummages through the items under the sink, finding cleaning supplies, spare toiletries, and, tucked in the back corner, an old, nearly empty box of tampons.  

  

Her hand freezes as she pulls the box out, her expression shifting from curiosity to confusion.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Tampons?  

  

She examines the box, noting its worn edges and faded branding.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Who?  

  

Her mind races, piecing together possibilities.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

An ex? Kathy? Someone else?  

  

She sets the box down carefully, her breath quickening.  

  

---

  

**Internal Conflict**  

  

Sherry closes the cabinet doors and stands, gripping the countertop.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

You’re overthinking this. It’s just an old box.  

  

Her gaze drifts to her reflection in the mirror, her expression tense.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But why keep it? Why not throw it out?  

  

Her thoughts shift darker, paranoia creeping in.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Has someone else been here? Recently?  

  

Her stomach tightens, and she glances toward the bathroom door, half expecting someone to walk in.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

No. Stop. You’re being ridiculous.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Decision**  

  

She takes a deep breath, forcing herself to calm down.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

You’re not going to ruin this. Not over some stupid box.  

  

She picks up the box again, shoving it back into the cabinet. Her movements are brisk, almost angry.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Just leave it alone.  

  

She stands, smoothing her hair and adjusting her expression before heading toward the door.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Focus on Jeff. On tonight. On what’s real.  

  

She opens the door, stepping back into the bedroom where Jeff waits, oblivious to her discovery.  

  

---


### **Scene 39: Rejoining Jeff**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s bedroom, late evening. Sherry reenters the room after her unsettling discovery in the bathroom. Jeff, lying casually on top of the blankets, has been anticipating her return. The warmth of his gaze contrasts with Sherry’s simmering unease, creating a subtle tension that underscores their growing dynamic.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – NIGHT**  

  

The room is bathed in a soft, golden glow from a bedside lamp. Jeff lies stretched out on the bed, the blankets rumpled beneath him. His hair is slightly tousled, and his expression is relaxed but eager as he watches the door.  

  

The door opens, and Sherry steps in, her expression carefully composed. Her damp hair clings to her neck, and she’s wearing one of Jeff’s oversized band t-shirts, the hem skimming her thighs.  

  

Jeff’s eyes light up, his voice low and playful.  

  

**JEFF**  

There she is.  

  

Sherry offers a faint smile, closing the door behind her.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Were you waiting long?  

  

Jeff shakes his head, his gaze sweeping over her.  

  

**JEFF**  

Worth the wait.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Perspective**  

  

The camera lingers on Jeff’s face as he takes her in, his admiration evident.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

Gorgeous. Like she doesn’t even know how stunning she is.  

  

His smirk softens into a more genuine smile.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

And she’s here. With me.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Perspective**  

  

The camera shifts to Sherry as she walks toward the bed. Her steps are slow, measured, her mind still racing.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s looking at you like you’re the only woman in the world.  

  

Her gaze flickers briefly to the nightstand, then back to Jeff.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

So why do you feel like a fraud?  

  

She forces a brighter smile, climbing onto the bed beside him.  

  

---

  

**Playful Banter**

**JEFF**  

You look good in my shirt.  

  

Sherry raises an eyebrow, her voice light but probing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Only good?  

  

Jeff chuckles, reaching out to trace a finger along her arm.  

  

**JEFF**  

Better than good.  

  

Sherry laughs softly, though her smile falters briefly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Careful, rock star. You’ll spoil me.  

  

**JEFF**  

That’s the idea.  

  

---

  

**Subtle Tension**  

  

As Jeff leans in, Sherry shifts slightly, her movements hesitant. He notices, pulling back just enough to study her face.  

  

**JEFF**  

You okay?  

  

Sherry nods quickly, her smile returning.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. Just… tired.  

  

Jeff’s brow furrows slightly, but he doesn’t press.  

  

**JEFF**  

Fair enough. Long day.  

  

Sherry nods, leaning into him and resting her head on his shoulder.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Affection**  

  

Jeff wraps an arm around her, his voice quieter now.  

  

**JEFF**  

You know, you’ve got this way of walking into a room and making it feel… better.  

  

Sherry tilts her head to look at him, her smile softening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s sweet.  

  

**JEFF**  

Just telling the truth.  

  

Sherry closes her eyes briefly, letting herself sink into the warmth of the moment.  

  

---

  

**Internal Struggles**  

  

The camera lingers on Sherry’s face as her expression shifts subtly, her thoughts spiraling again.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s sweet now. But what about tomorrow? Or the next day?  

  

Her gaze drifts to the dresser, then back to Jeff.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

And what’s with that box? Why is it still here?  

  

Jeff’s voice breaks through her thoughts.  

  

**JEFF**  

Penny for your thoughts?  

  

Sherry forces a small laugh, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Just thinking how lucky I am to be here.  

  

Jeff smiles, leaning down to kiss her forehead.  

  

**JEFF**  

We’re both lucky.  

  

---

### **Scene 40: The Intimate Evening Continues**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s bedroom, late evening. The warmth of their connection contrasts with Sherry’s nagging thoughts about the tampon box and her growing insecurities. Jeff, still in a playful and romantic mood, surprises Sherry with a spontaneous and extravagant idea: a trip to Pago Pago. Sherry struggles to balance his enthusiasm with her need to process her feelings, finding a way to calm him while maintaining her composure.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – NIGHT**  

  

Jeff lies back against the pillows, his arm draped casually over Sherry’s waist. The soft glow of the bedside lamp casts a golden light on their relaxed forms. Sherry nestles against him, her fingers absently tracing patterns on his chest.  

  

Jeff tilts his head, looking down at her with a grin.  

  

**JEFF**  

You ever been to Pago Pago?  

  

Sherry’s hand pauses mid-motion, her brow furrowing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Pago Pago? Like… American Samoa?  

  

Jeff nods, his grin widening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. Thought we could go next month. Just you and me.  

  

Sherry sits up slightly, her expression a mix of surprise and uncertainty.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Next month?  

  

Jeff props himself up on one elbow, his tone playful.  

  

**JEFF**  

Why not? Sun, sand, no one to bother us.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Internal Conflict**  

  

Sherry forces a smile, her mind racing.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Pago Pago? Is he serious?  

  

Her gaze flickers to Jeff’s hopeful expression, and her chest tightens.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s serious.  

  

She brushes a strand of hair behind her ear, stalling for time.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s… spontaneous.  

  

Jeff chuckles, leaning closer.  

  

**JEFF**  

That’s the point. No schedules, no stress. Just us.  

  

Sherry’s smile wavers, her tone light but hesitant.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Sounds amazing.  

  

**JEFF**  

It will be.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Attempt to Slow Things Down**  

  

Sherry shifts, sitting up fully and turning to face him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff, you know I’d love that. But… next month?  

  

Jeff raises an eyebrow, his tone teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

You’ve got plans?  

  

Sherry laughs softly, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

No, but I’ve got work. And kids. And a million other things to juggle.  

  

Jeff sits up, his expression softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

You can take a break. You deserve it.  

  

Sherry hesitates, her fingers fidgeting with the hem of her borrowed t-shirt.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I don’t know. It’s just… a lot to think about.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Persistence**  

  

Jeff reaches out, taking her hands in his.  

  

**JEFF**  

Sherry, you work hard. You’re always putting everyone else first. Let me do this for you. For us.  

  

Sherry’s eyes meet his, and she feels a pang of guilt.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s so earnest. So sure.  

  

Her gaze flickers to his hands holding hers, then back to his face.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But I need time.  

  

---

  

**Sherry Finds a Middle Ground**  

  

Sherry squeezes his hands gently, her tone softening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Tell you what. Let me think about it.  

  

Jeff tilts his head, studying her.  

  

**JEFF**  

Think about it?  

  

Sherry nods, offering a faint smile.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. I just need to make sure everything at home is squared away first.  

  

Jeff’s expression relaxes, and he smiles.  

  

**JEFF**  

Okay. But don’t think too long. Pago Pago’s waiting.  

  

Sherry laughs, leaning in to kiss him lightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I’ll keep that in mind.  

  

---

  

**Nagging Thoughts Persist**  

  

As Jeff pulls her back down onto the bed, his hands roaming her waist, Sherry closes her eyes, trying to let herself get lost in the moment.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s wonderful. Thoughtful.  

  

Her mind flashes briefly to the tampon box and the portrait of Kathy.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But what else is he hiding?  

  

She exhales softly, opening her eyes to look at him.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

For now, focus on us. Just us.  

  

Jeff grins down at her, his tone teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

You know, Pago Pago would be even better with you there.  

  

Sherry laughs again, this time more genuinely, and pulls him closer.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Let’s see how tonight goes first, rock star.

### **Scene 41: Sherry’s Reflections**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s bedroom, late night. Sherry lies awake beside Jeff, grappling with her doubts and fears. While Jeff appears relaxed and expectant, she struggles to balance her need for clarity with her desire to give him a satisfying and intimate conclusion to their evening. Her internal conflict grows as she wrestles with her feelings, ultimately deciding on a way to keep the night from spiraling further.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – NIGHT**  

  

The soft light from the bedside lamp casts warm shadows over the room. Jeff lies on his side, propped up on one elbow, his gaze fixed on Sherry. She’s lying on her back, staring at the ceiling, her expression distant.  

  

**JEFF**  

You okay?  

  

Sherry blinks, turning her head to look at him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. Just… thinking.  

  

Jeff smirks, reaching out to trace a finger along her arm.  

  

**JEFF**  

Thinking’s overrated.  

  

Sherry chuckles softly, though it lacks her usual warmth.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Maybe.

**JEFF**  

You sure you’re okay?  

  

Sherry forces a smile, nodding.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I’m fine.

**Internal Conflict**  

  

As Jeff leans back against the pillows, Sherry’s gaze shifts to the ceiling again. Her mind races, her thoughts a jumble of doubt and determination.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Fine. That’s what you say when you don’t want to explain. When you’re trying to convince yourself everything’s okay.  

  

Her chest tightens as flashes of the evening play in her mind: the portrait, the tampon box, Jeff’s eager mention of Pago Pago.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

It’s too much. Too fast.  

  

She glances at Jeff out of the corner of her eye, noting his relaxed posture and easy smile.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But he’s here. He’s trying.  

  

Her jaw tightens, and she inhales deeply, forcing herself to focus.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He deserves something.  

  

---

  

**Searching for a Solution**  

  

Sherry sits up slightly, adjusting the hem of the oversized shirt she’s wearing.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Think, Sherry. What does he need? What can you do?  

  

She glances at Jeff again, her gaze softening.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s always giving. Always trying to make me feel special.  

  

Her mind flashes to their earlier moments: his laughter, his touch, his quiet admiration.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe tonight should be about him.  

  

---

  

**Tamping Down the Fears**  

  

Sherry exhales slowly, shaking her head as if to clear it.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Forget the portrait. Forget the tampons.  

  

Her hands clench briefly in her lap before she releases them.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

For now, just… let it go.  

  

She leans down, brushing her fingers lightly over Jeff’s chest.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Hey.  

  

Jeff glances at her, his expression softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Hey yourself.  

  

Sherry smiles faintly, her voice quieter.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’ve been so good to me. Maybe it’s time I return the favor.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Reaction**  

  

Jeff raises an eyebrow, his smirk returning.  

  

**JEFF**  

Oh?  

  

Sherry nods, leaning closer until their faces are just inches apart.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Just… let me take care of you tonight.  

  

Jeff’s grin widens, and he reaches up to tuck a strand of hair behind her ear.  

  

**JEFF**  

You already do, Sherry.  

  

Sherry’s heart twists at his words, but she pushes the feeling down, focusing instead on the moment.  

  

---

### **Scene 42: Jeff’s Perspective**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s bedroom, late night. Jeff lies with Sherry, fully immersed in the moment, feeling emotionally and physically ready to deepen their connection. As Sherry reaches for lubricant, Jeff’s thoughts reveal his eagerness to show her his world and his desire to forge a deeper bond, both intimately and emotionally.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – NIGHT**  

  

The golden glow of the bedside lamp casts warm shadows across the room. Jeff lies on his back, his hand resting gently on Sherry’s waist as she leans over the nightstand. Her movements are deliberate but unhurried, the tension between them charged with quiet anticipation.  

  

Jeff watches her, his gaze tender yet hungry.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

God, she’s gorgeous. Everything about her… the way she moves, the way she looks at me.  

  

Sherry retrieves a small bottle of lubricant, her fingers brushing against his hand as she turns back toward him. Jeff feels a warmth spread through his chest, his voice soft when he speaks.  

  

**JEFF**  

You okay?  

  

Sherry nods, her smile faint but reassuring.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah.

Jeff nods, his tone growing more reflective.  

  

**JEFF**

His gaze meets hers, his voice quieter now.  

  

**JEFF**

Sherry’s smile fades slightly, her expression thoughtful.  

  

**SHERRY**

**JEFF (V.O.)**

**The Moment Deepens**  

  

Jeff leans in, his lips brushing against hers as his hand trails down her back.  

  

**JEFF**  

You’re something else, Sherry.

**SHERRY**  

So are you, rock star.  

  

Jeff’s grin widens, and he pulls her closer, the tension between them building as the camera pans away, leaving their intimacy to the imagination.

### **Scene 43: Sherry’s Self-Reflection and Confrontation**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s mansion bathroom, late night. After an intense moment of intimacy with Jeff, Sherry finds herself alone, washing her hands and reflecting on their connection. The stark contrast between their lives—his wealth, fame, and charm, and her grounded but complicated world—sparks doubt. As she processes her thoughts, she decides to confront Jeff directly about whether he sees her as a conquest, a conversation fraught with vulnerability and honesty.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BATHROOM – NIGHT**  

  

Sherry stands at the marble sink, the water running over her hands. Her hair is slightly damp from exertion, her cheeks flushed. She stares at the flowing water, her thoughts racing.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

This isn’t real.  

  

Her gaze shifts to her reflection in the oversized mirror, her expression a mix of wonder and apprehension.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Or is it?  

  

She shuts off the water and dries her hands with a plush towel, glancing around the opulent bathroom.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

A place like this. A man like him. What am I even doing here?  

  

Her eyes flicker toward the cabinet under the sink. She takes a hesitant step toward it before stopping herself, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

No. Not again. You don’t need more questions right now.  

  

She grips the edge of the sink, her knuckles white.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But what if I’m just another name on his list?  

  

Her shoulders tense, and she exhales sharply, forcing herself to calm down.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

If I don’t ask, I’ll never know.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – NIGHT**  

  

Jeff lies sprawled across the bed, his head resting on one hand, his expression relaxed. He looks up as Sherry reenters the room, her movements slower, more deliberate.  

  

**JEFF**  

Hey.  

  

Sherry offers a faint smile, crossing her arms as she approaches the bed.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Hey.  

  

Jeff sits up slightly, his brow furrowing.  

  

**JEFF**  

Everything okay?  

  

Sherry hesitates, her fingers gripping the hem of her borrowed shirt.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Can I ask you something?  

  

Jeff’s smile softens, and he nods.  

  

**JEFF**  

Of course.  

  

---

  

**The Confrontation**  

  

Sherry sits on the edge of the bed, her gaze focused on her hands.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Do you…  

  

She pauses, exhaling deeply before continuing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Do you see me as a conquest?  

  

Jeff blinks, his expression shifting to surprise.  

  

**JEFF**  

A conquest?  

  

Sherry nods, her voice quieter now.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. Like… another notch in your belt.  

  

Jeff leans forward, his tone serious.  

  

**JEFF**  

Sherry, no. That’s not how I see you.  

  

She looks up, her eyes searching his face.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re sure?  

  

Jeff reaches out, taking her hands in his.  

  

**JEFF**  

I’m sure. You’re not a conquest. You’re… different.  

  

Sherry’s lips twitch into a faint smile, but her doubt lingers.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Different how?  

  

Jeff hesitates, choosing his words carefully.  

  

**JEFF**  

Because you make me feel like I can be myself. Not the rock star, not the guy everyone expects. Just… Jeff.  

  

Sherry’s chest tightens at his words, her voice soft.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I want to believe that.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Reassurance**  

  

Jeff squeezes her hands gently, his gaze steady.  

  

**JEFF**  

I’m not perfect, Sherry. I’ve made mistakes. But I wouldn’t be here with you if I didn’t want this to mean something.  

  

Sherry exhales slowly, her shoulders relaxing slightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I just… I need this to feel safe.  

  

Jeff nods, his tone gentle.  

  

**JEFF**  

Then we’ll make it safe. Together.  

  

Sherry studies him for a moment before nodding, her smile returning, more genuine this time.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay.  

  

Jeff grins, leaning forward to kiss her forehead.  

  

**JEFF**  

Okay.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Resolution**  

  

As Jeff pulls her into a warm embrace, Sherry closes her eyes, her thoughts quieter now.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe he’s not perfect. Maybe I’m not either. But for now… this is enough.
