### **Scene 44: Sherry Processes the Conversation**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s bedroom, late night. After their heartfelt conversation, Jeff spoons Sherry, wrapping her in his warmth and leaving her to her thoughts in the deep silence of the room. Sherry reflects on her behavior and the emotional turbulence of the evening. Eventually, she clears her throat, breaking the silence and opening up about her inner turmoil, seeking to navigate the complex feelings swirling within her.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – NIGHT**  

  

The room is still, the only sound the faint crackle of the fireplace in the corner. Jeff lies behind Sherry, one arm draped over her waist, his breathing slow and steady. His warmth envelops her, but her mind is anything but calm.  

  

Sherry stares at the faint shadows on the wall, her eyes wide open.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

This isn’t how tonight was supposed to go.  

  

Her gaze shifts to Jeff’s hand resting on her waist, the weight of it grounding her.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

I wanted to be confident. Cool. Like I had it all together.  

  

Her lips press into a thin line as her thoughts spiral.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Instead, I spiraled. Again.  

  

---

  

**Reflecting on Her Actions**  

  

Sherry exhales softly, her chest rising and falling in time with Jeff’s behind her.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

First, I go through his bathroom. Again. Like I’m looking for something to be upset about.  

  

Her gaze lowers, focusing on the faint outline of their legs tangled under the blanket.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Then I come back here and ask if I’m just another conquest.  

  

Her stomach tightens, and she swallows hard.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

What kind of woman does that?  

  

Jeff shifts slightly behind her, his arm tightening around her waist. Sherry stiffens momentarily before relaxing again.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He deserves better than that.  

  

---

  

**Breaking the Silence**  

  

The unbearable silence stretches on, pressing down on Sherry. Finally, she clears her throat, her voice quiet but steady.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff?  

  

He stirs slightly, his voice drowsy but attentive.  

  

**JEFF**  

Hmm?  

  

Sherry hesitates, her gaze fixed on the wall.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Can I… say something?  

  

Jeff shifts behind her, propping himself up slightly.  

  

**JEFF**  

Of course.  

  

---

  

**Opening Up**  

  

Sherry takes a deep breath, her fingers twisting the edge of the blanket.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I don’t know what’s wrong with me tonight.  

  

Jeff’s brow furrows, his tone gentle.  

  

**JEFF**  

Nothing’s wrong with you.  

  

Sherry laughs softly, though it’s laced with bitterness.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Feels like there is.  

  

She turns slightly to look at him, her expression vulnerable.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I keep second-guessing everything. Myself. You. Us.  

  

Jeff’s hand moves to her shoulder, his touch reassuring.  

  

**JEFF**  

That’s okay.  

  

Sherry shakes her head, her voice trembling slightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

No, it’s not. You’ve been nothing but sweet, and I…  

  

She trails off, biting her lip.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I keep making it harder than it needs to be.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Response**  

  

Jeff shifts closer, his tone steady.  

  

**JEFF**  

Sherry, it’s okay to feel unsure. To ask questions.  

  

She glances at him, her brow furrowing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Even when it’s every five minutes?  

  

Jeff smiles faintly, his tone softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Even then.  

  

Sherry studies his face for a moment before turning back toward the wall, her thoughts quieter now.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s patient. Too patient.  

  

---

  

**Coping with the Currents**  

  

Sherry closes her eyes briefly, letting out a slow breath.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I think… I just need time.  

  

Jeff nods, his voice calm.  

  

**JEFF**  

Take all the time you need.  

  

She turns back toward him, her expression softening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Thank you.  

  

Jeff leans down, pressing a kiss to her forehead.  

  

**JEFF**  

For what?  

  

Sherry smiles faintly, her voice quieter.  

  

**SHERRY**  

For being you.  

  

---

  

**The Dynamic Evolves**  

  

Jeff settles back down, pulling her closer into his embrace. Sherry nestles against him, her tension easing slightly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe I don’t have to figure it all out tonight.  

  

Her gaze drifts back to the wall, her thoughts slowing.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe… just being here is enough. For now.  

  

The room falls silent again, but the tension has shifted, replaced by a tentative sense of peace.  

  

---


### **Scene 45: Morning Reflections and Sisterly Boasting**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s mansion, early morning. Sherry wakes up tender and sore, feeling a mix of physical satisfaction and emotional reflection. While Jeff remains sound asleep, she decides to call her sister, eager to share her experience and process the whirlwind of feelings.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – EARLY MORNING**  

  

Soft light filters through the floor-to-ceiling windows, casting a warm glow over the bedroom. Jeff is sprawled out under the blankets, his breathing deep and even. Sherry lies on her side, watching him for a moment before shifting slightly, wincing with a small smile.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Tender and sore. In the best way possible.  

  

She stretches carefully, her body humming with the memories of the night before. Her fingers brush against Jeff’s arm, and she pauses, studying his peaceful expression.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He looks so… calm. Like none of this is new to him.  

  

Her gaze drifts toward the ceiling, her mind racing.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

For me, it’s like stepping into a dream I didn’t know I had.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Inner Conflict**  

  

Sherry shifts again, sitting up carefully and glancing toward the clock on the nightstand.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

And yet, it’s not just the fun. It’s everything else. The questions, the doubts.  

  

Her brow furrows briefly, but the corners of her mouth tug upward.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But damn, it’s been fun.  

  

She glances back at Jeff, her smile softening.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

So much fun.  

  

---

  

**Reaching Out**  

  

Sherry picks up her phone from the nightstand and tiptoes out of bed, careful not to wake Jeff. She wraps herself in a robe hanging on the back of a nearby chair and pads into the living room, settling onto the plush couch.  

  

She scrolls through her contacts and dials her sister.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S SISTER’S KITCHEN – EARLY MORNING**  

  

Sherry’s sister sits at the kitchen table, a steaming mug of coffee in hand. Her phone buzzes, and she sighs, picking it up.  

  

**SISTER**  

(resigned)  

Of course.  

  

She answers, her voice drowsy but amused.  

  

**SISTER**  

It’s not even 5 AM. This better be good.  

  

---

  

**Split-Screen: SHERRY IN LIVING ROOM / SISTER IN KITCHEN**  

  

Sherry grins, her voice bright.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Oh, it is.  

  

Her sister raises an eyebrow, sipping her coffee.  

  

**SISTER**  

Let me guess. You’re calling to brag.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Not brag. Just… share.  

  

**SISTER**  

Uh-huh.  

  

Sherry leans back against the couch, her smile widening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay, maybe a little bragging.  

  

Her sister laughs softly, shaking her head.  

  

**SISTER**  

Spill.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Boast**  

  

Sherry tilts her head back, her tone teasing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Let’s just say last night was… everything.  

  

Her sister smirks, leaning forward.  

  

**SISTER**  

Details.  

  

Sherry hesitates, glancing toward the hallway leading to the bedroom.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I mean, it’s not like I’m going to give you a play-by-play.  

  

**SISTER**  

No, but you’re dying to tell me something.  

  

Sherry laughs, covering her face briefly with her hand.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Fine. He’s… amazing. Sweet, thoughtful, and… wow.  

  

Her sister chuckles, taking another sip of coffee.  

  

**SISTER**  

Wow, huh?  

  

**SHERRY**  

Oh, yeah.  

  

---

  

**Processing the Moment**  

  

Sherry’s tone softens, her smile fading slightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

It’s just… a lot, you know?  

  

Her sister’s expression grows more serious.  

  

**SISTER**  

What do you mean?  

  

**SHERRY**  

I mean, he’s this big rock star. His life is so different from mine. And yet…  

  

She trails off, her voice quieter.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I feel like I belong when I’m with him.  

  

Her sister leans back, her tone thoughtful.  

  

**SISTER**  

That’s not a bad thing, Sherry.  

  

**SHERRY**  

No, it’s not. It’s just… unexpected.  

  

---

  

**Playful Teasing**  

  

Her sister smirks again, her tone lightening.  

  

**SISTER**  

So, when do I get to meet this rock star of yours?  

  

Sherry laughs, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Not anytime soon.  

  

**SISTER**  

Why not? Afraid he won’t live up to my expectations?  

  

Sherry grins, her voice teasing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

More like I’m afraid *you* won’t live up to *his.*  

  

Her sister laughs, rolling her eyes.  

  

**SISTER**  

Touché.  

  

---

  

**Ending the Call**  

  

Sherry glances toward the hallway again, her expression softening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I should go. He’s still asleep, and I want to be there when he wakes up.  

  

Her sister nods, her smile warm.  

  

**SISTER**  

Enjoy it, Sherry. You deserve this.  

  

Sherry’s smile widens, her voice quiet but firm.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Thanks.  

  

She ends the call, setting her phone down and staring out the window for a moment, the snow-covered gorge glowing in the early morning light.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Maybe I do deserve this.  

  

---

### **Scene 46: Quiet Morning Connection**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s bedroom, early morning. Sherry sits beside Jeff as he sleeps, her gaze lingering on his relaxed form. The quiet intimacy of the moment allows her to reflect on their connection. When Jeff stirs and wakes to find her by his side, the tender exchange deepens their bond.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – EARLY MORNING**  

  

The room is serene, bathed in the soft glow of dawn filtering through the large windows. Jeff lies sprawled on his side, his breathing steady, the faintest hint of a smile tugging at his lips even in sleep.  

  

Sherry sits cross-legged beside him, wrapped in an oversized robe, her hair tousled from the night before. Her gaze lingers on Jeff’s face, tracing the curve of his jaw, the tousle of his hair, the peacefulness in his expression.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

How does someone like him even exist?  

  

Her fingers rest lightly on her lap, trembling slightly as she processes her thoughts.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

This brilliant, complicated man who makes me feel like I’m the only person in the world.  

  

She tilts her head, her expression softening as her eyes drift lower to his chest rising and falling rhythmically under the blanket.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He looks so calm. So… human.  

  

Her lips curve into a faint smile, and she leans forward slightly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

And he chose me.  

  

---

  

**The Moment of Stillness**  

  

Sherry exhales softly, her breath barely audible as she straightens. She tucks a strand of hair behind her ear, her gaze never leaving Jeff.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

I could sit here forever.  

  

Her hand hesitates over his shoulder, but she doesn’t touch him, savoring the stillness of the moment.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

This is real. For now, it’s real.  

  

---

  

**Jeff Wakes**  

  

Jeff stirs, his brow furrowing slightly as he shifts under the blanket. His eyes flutter open, squinting briefly against the soft light. He blinks, his gaze landing on Sherry. A slow, sleepy smile spreads across his face.  

  

**JEFF**  

Hey.  

  

Sherry’s smile widens, her voice soft.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Hey.  

  

Jeff props himself up on one elbow, his hair sticking up at odd angles.  

  

**JEFF**  

How long have you been sitting there?  

  

Sherry shrugs, her tone playful.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Long enough.  

  

Jeff chuckles, running a hand through his hair.  

  

**JEFF**  

You should’ve woken me.  

  

Sherry tilts her head, her gaze warm.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You looked too peaceful.  

  

Jeff reaches out, his fingers brushing against her arm.  

  

**JEFF**  

So do you.  

  

---

  

**Their Connection Deepens**  

  

Sherry laughs softly, leaning into his touch.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Not after last night. I’m pretty sure I’m a mess.  

  

Jeff smirks, his voice low and teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

A beautiful mess.  

  

Sherry rolls her eyes, though her cheeks flush slightly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re ridiculous.  

  

Jeff’s grin softens, and he shifts closer, resting his forehead against hers.  

  

**JEFF**  

Maybe. But I mean it.  

  

Sherry closes her eyes briefly, letting out a soft breath.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s impossible. And perfect.  

  

---

  

**The Tender Moment**  

  

Jeff leans back, his hand trailing down her arm before resting on her hand.  

  

**JEFF**  

You okay?  

  

Sherry nods, her voice quiet but steady.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. Just… thinking.  

  

Jeff raises an eyebrow, his tone light.  

  

**JEFF**  

About?  

  

Sherry hesitates, her gaze drifting toward the window before returning to him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

About how lucky I am.  

  

Jeff smiles, his voice softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Me too.  

  

---
### **Scene 47: Morning Routine and Plans**  

**Setting**: Jeff’s mansion, early morning. The morning sun shines over the snow-covered landscape as Sherry and Jeff discuss their plans for the day. Sherry has a mix of indulgent and adventurous ideas, while Jeff adds his own suggestion of visiting the Air Force Museum. Their playful dynamic and growing connection unfold as they move through their morning routine together.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – EARLY MORNING**  

  

Jeff and Sherry are still tangled in the blankets, the warmth of the room contrasting with the snowy scene visible through the large windows. Sherry stretches, letting out a contented sigh as Jeff props himself up on one elbow, watching her with a lazy grin.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay, rock star. What’s the plan for today?  

  

Jeff chuckles, reaching out to brush a strand of hair from her face.  

  

**JEFF**  

You tell me.  

  

Sherry sits up, pulling the blanket around her shoulders as she ticks off her ideas on her fingers.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Breakfast. Shower. Sex. And maybe a walk down to that gorge.  

  

Jeff raises an eyebrow, his grin widening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Ambitious.  

  

Sherry smirks, glancing over her shoulder at him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Think you can keep up?  

  

**JEFF**  

Oh, I’m game.  

  

He sits up, stretching his arms over his head.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

And while we’re being ambitious… how about a quick trip to the Air Force Museum? It’s just up the road.  

  

Sherry tilts her head, intrigued.  

  

**SHERRY**  

The Air Force Museum?  

  

Jeff nods, his tone light.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. You’ll love it. Planes, history, a little inspiration.  

  

Sherry laughs softly, leaning back against the headboard.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Sounds like fun. But first, breakfast.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S KITCHEN – MORNING**  

  

The kitchen is spacious and modern, with sleek countertops and high-end appliances. Jeff stands at the stove, flipping pancakes, while Sherry leans against the counter, sipping a cup of coffee.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You cook?  

  

Jeff glances over his shoulder, smirking.  

  

**JEFF**  

I can handle pancakes. Don’t ask for anything fancy.  

  

Sherry chuckles, setting her mug down and stepping closer.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Pancakes are a good start.  

  

Jeff slides a pancake onto a plate and hands it to her, his grin teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

You’re easy to please.  

  

Sherry raises an eyebrow, her tone playful.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Don’t get cocky.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BATHROOM – LATER**  

  

Steam fills the bathroom as Sherry and Jeff step into the oversized glass shower. The water cascades over them, and their laughter echoes in the space.  

  

**SHERRY**  

This shower is bigger than my bedroom.  

  

Jeff chuckles, reaching for the shampoo.  

  

**JEFF**  

Perks of rock stardom.  

  

Sherry tilts her head, her smile softening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Must be nice.  

  

Jeff glances at her, his tone light but sincere.  

  

**JEFF**  

It has its moments.  

  

They share a quiet moment, the sound of the water filling the space as they wash away the remnants of the night.  

  

---

  

**INT. JEFF’S BEDROOM – LATER**  

  

Jeff and Sherry tumble back onto the bed, their laughter giving way to a deeper intimacy. The camera pans away as their connection deepens once more, leaving the details to the imagination.  

  

---

  

**EXT. LITTLE MIAMI RIVER GORGE – MORNING**  

  

Sherry and Jeff walk along the snowy path leading down to the river gorge. Sherry is bundled in a coat and scarf, her breath visible in the crisp air. Jeff walks beside her, pointing out the sights.  

  

**JEFF**  

Spring’s amazing here. The trees fill out, the water runs fast… it’s like a whole different world.  

  

Sherry glances at him, her expression soft.  

  

**SHERRY**  

It’s beautiful now.  

  

Jeff smiles, nudging her playfully.  

  

**JEFF**  

Wait till you see it with green everywhere.  

  

---

  

**INT. CAR – LATER**  

  

Jeff and Sherry drive north, the snowy Ohio countryside rolling past the windows. Jeff taps his fingers on the steering wheel in time with the music playing softly on the radio.  

  

**SHERRY**  

So, why the Air Force Museum?  

  

Jeff shrugs, glancing at her with a grin.  

  

**JEFF**  

I like planes. Always have.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(raising an eyebrow)  

Planes?  

  

Jeff nods, his tone light.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yep. And there’s this bomber there—Bockscar—it dropped the second nuke. Fascinating piece of history.  

  

Sherry’s eyes widen slightly, her tone teasing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You really are full of surprises.  

  

Jeff chuckles, his grin widening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Stick with me. You’ll learn a lot.  

  

---

### **Scene 48: The Air Force Museum Visit**  

**Setting**: The National Museum of the U.S. Air Force, mid-morning. Jeff and Sherry stroll through the cavernous museum, surrounded by towering aircraft and exhibits steeped in history. Jeff, eager to impress and share his knowledge, occasionally lets his enthusiasm override his emotional awareness. Sherry quickly recognizes that his excitement, though occasionally condescending, reveals a more genuine side of him that she hadn’t fully seen before.  

  

---

  

**INT. AIR FORCE MUSEUM – WWII EXHIBIT – MORNING**  

  

Jeff and Sherry walk hand-in-hand through the museum, the polished floors reflecting the massive planes suspended overhead. Jeff’s face lights up as they approach a sleek, silver bomber.  

  

**JEFF**  

There it is—Bockscar.  

  

Sherry glances at the plaque, tilting her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s the one you mentioned in the car, right?  

  

Jeff nods, his tone reverent.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. It dropped the second atomic bomb on Nagasaki.  

  

He gestures toward the plane, his voice growing more animated.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

It’s crazy to think about. A plane like this, carrying something so powerful, so destructive. And the crew—they weren’t even sure it would work.  

  

Sherry studies the plane, her expression thoughtful.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s… a lot to process.  

  

Jeff nods, stepping closer to the exhibit.  

  

**JEFF**  

It’s a turning point in history. The war ended, but at what cost?  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s First Misstep**  

  

He glances back at Sherry, his tone shifting slightly.  

  

**JEFF**  

I mean, it’s not like most people think about these things.  

  

Sherry raises an eyebrow, her lips curving into a faint smirk.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Most people?  

  

Jeff hesitates, his grin faltering.  

  

**JEFF**  

I didn’t mean it like that. Just…  

  

Sherry chuckles, stepping closer to him.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Relax, professor. I’m following you.  

  

Jeff’s grin returns, though his cheeks flush slightly.  

  

---

  

**INT. AIR FORCE MUSEUM – COLD WAR EXHIBIT – LATER**  

  

Jeff and Sherry walk through a section filled with Cold War-era aircraft. Jeff gestures toward a towering black jet, his voice filled with awe.  

  

**JEFF**  

That’s the SR-71 Blackbird. Fastest plane ever built.  

  

Sherry looks up, her eyes widening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

It’s huge.  

  

Jeff nods, his tone picking up again.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah, and it flew higher than anything else. They used it for reconnaissance—spying on the Soviets, mostly. And no one could touch it.  

  

He pauses, glancing at her.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

You probably didn’t know that, huh?  

  

Sherry raises both eyebrows this time, folding her arms.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Oh, I didn’t?  

  

Jeff’s smile freezes, and he rubs the back of his neck.  

  

**JEFF**  

I—uh… I mean, not everyone knows.  

  

---

  

**Sherry Recognizes Jeff’s Excitement**  

  

Sherry laughs softly, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff, you’re so excited you’re tripping over your own words.  

  

Jeff blinks, tilting his head.  

  

**JEFF**  

I am?  

  

Sherry nods, stepping closer and placing a hand on his arm.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. It’s kind of adorable.  

  

Jeff frowns slightly, his tone self-deprecating.  

  

**JEFF**  

I don’t mean to sound… like that.  

  

Sherry smiles, squeezing his arm.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You don’t. Not really.  

  

She glances back at the plane, her expression softening.  

  

**SHERRY (CONT’D)**  

You’re just passionate. And that’s not a bad thing.  

  

Jeff studies her for a moment, his expression relaxing.  

  

**JEFF**  

Thanks.  

  

---

  

**INT. AIR FORCE MUSEUM – SPACE EXHIBIT – LATER**  

  

Jeff and Sherry walk through the dimly lit space exhibit, surrounded by models of rockets and lunar modules. Jeff’s voice softens, his excitement tempered but still genuine.  

  

**JEFF**  

You know, the astronauts used to look at the Earth from space and call it the “pale blue dot.”  

  

Sherry glances at him, her tone curious.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s poetic.  

  

Jeff smiles faintly, his gaze fixed on a model of the Apollo lunar module.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. I guess even guys in space get sentimental.  

  

Sherry laughs softly, leaning into his side.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You would’ve fit right in.  

  

Jeff chuckles, wrapping an arm around her shoulders.  

  

**JEFF**  

I don’t know about that. I’m not great with enclosed spaces.  

  

Sherry tilts her head, studying him with a smile.  

  

**SHERRY**  

But you are great with stories.  

  

Jeff’s smile widens, and he presses a kiss to her temple.  

  

**JEFF**  

Thanks.  

  

---

### **Scene 49: Continuing the Day**  

**Setting**: Jeff and Sherry leave the Air Force Museum, energized by their visit. They head to a nearby diner for lunch, where their playful dynamic continues to unfold. The day shifts as they explore more of the wintery Ohio countryside, culminating in a quiet, reflective moment by the Little Miami River gorge.  

  

---

  

**EXT. AIR FORCE MUSEUM – PARKING LOT – LATE MORNING**  

  

Jeff and Sherry step out into the brisk air, their breath visible as they laugh about a particularly odd exhibit they saw. Sherry zips up her coat, her cheeks flushed from both the cold and their conversation.  

  

**JEFF**  

Did you see that simulator? The thing looked like it came out of a bad sci-fi movie.  

  

Sherry grins, nodding.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I was half expecting it to start smoking when they turned it on.  

  

Jeff chuckles, unlocking the car and opening the passenger door for her.  

  

**JEFF**  

You’re braver than me if you ever get in one of those.  

  

Sherry slides into the car, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Not a chance.  

  

---

  

**INT. DINER – EARLY AFTERNOON**  

  

The diner is cozy and bustling, with the sound of clinking dishes and soft chatter filling the air. Sherry and Jeff sit across from each other in a red vinyl booth, steam rising from their coffee mugs.  

  

Jeff leans back, glancing at the menu.  

  

**JEFF**  

What’s the move? Pancakes again?  

  

Sherry smirks, setting her menu down.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re really stuck on pancakes today, huh?  

  

Jeff shrugs, grinning.  

  

**JEFF**  

It’s a theme.  

  

Sherry laughs, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I think I’m going for the burger. Gotta balance out all the museum walking.  

  

Jeff raises an eyebrow, his tone teasing.  

  

**JEFF**  

That’s quite a leap from pancakes.  

  

Sherry leans forward, resting her chin on her hand.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Don’t knock it till you try it.  

  

---

  

**Playful Banter**  

  

The waitress approaches, a friendly smile on her face.  

  

**WAITRESS**  

What can I get you folks?  

  

Sherry smiles, her tone light.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Burger and fries for me, please.  

  

Jeff nods, his grin widening.  

  

**JEFF**  

And pancakes. With extra syrup.  

  

Sherry raises an eyebrow, leaning back in her seat.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You’re really committed to this pancake thing.  

  

Jeff chuckles, handing the menus to the waitress.  

  

**JEFF**  

You’ve gotta admire consistency.  

  

The waitress laughs softly, walking away with their order.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(pretending to be serious)  

I don’t know if I should admire it or be concerned.  

  

Jeff smirks, reaching across the table to take her hand.  

  

**JEFF**  

Stick around. You’ll figure it out.  

  

---

  

**EXT. LITTLE MIAMI RIVER GORGE – MID-AFTERNOON**  

  

Snow crunches underfoot as Jeff and Sherry walk along the path leading to the gorge. The sun glints off the frozen river, and the bare trees cast intricate shadows over the ground.  

  

Jeff stops, gesturing toward the view.  

  

**JEFF**  

This is it.  

  

Sherry takes a moment, her breath visible as she exhales.  

  

**SHERRY**  

It’s beautiful.  

  

Jeff nods, his tone quieter now.  

  

**JEFF**  

I used to come here a lot. Just to think.  

  

Sherry glances at him, her expression softening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

What about?  

  

Jeff shrugs, his gaze fixed on the river.  

  

**JEFF**  

Everything. Nothing. It’s peaceful here.  

  

---

  

**A Quiet Moment**  

  

Sherry steps closer, slipping her arm through his.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I can see why you like it.  

  

Jeff looks down at her, his expression thoughtful.  

  

**JEFF**  

Thanks for coming today.  

  

Sherry tilts her head, her smile faint.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Thanks for inviting me.  

  

They stand in silence for a moment, the wind rustling through the trees around them.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Reflection**  

  

As they start walking again, Sherry glances at Jeff, her voice hesitant.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Do you ever feel… overwhelmed? By everything?  

  

Jeff raises an eyebrow, his tone curious.  

  

**JEFF**  

Like what?  

  

Sherry shrugs, looking ahead.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Life. Expectations. All of it.  

  

Jeff is quiet for a moment before nodding.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. A lot more than I let on.  

  

Sherry glances at him, her expression softening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You don’t have to keep it all in, you know.  

  

Jeff smiles faintly, squeezing her arm gently.  

  

**JEFF**  

Maybe not with you.  

  

Sherry’s chest tightens slightly, and she smiles back, her voice soft.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Good.  

  

---

### **Scene 50: Jeff's Emotional Brain Dump**  

**Setting**: Little Miami River gorge, mid-afternoon. As Jeff and Sherry continue their walk, Jeff’s thoughts and emotions overflow. Feeling deeply at ease with Sherry, he starts sharing everything on his mind—his joy, his comfort, his family, and how profoundly she has affected his life. Sherry listens intently, surprised and touched by the rawness of his honesty.  

  

---

  

**EXT. LITTLE MIAMI RIVER GORGE – MID-AFTERNOON**  

  

The snow crunches underfoot as Jeff and Sherry walk along the gorge. The air is crisp, their breath visible as they meander through the quiet, wintery landscape. Jeff’s gaze drifts to the frozen river, a pensive smile playing on his lips.  

  

**JEFF**  

You know…  

  

Sherry glances at him, tilting her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Hmm?  

  

Jeff hesitates, his tone softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

I’ve been thinking about how the last six weeks have felt.  

  

Sherry slows her pace slightly, sensing the shift in his tone.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Good things, I hope?  

  

Jeff nods, his voice gaining momentum.  

  

**JEFF**  

Good doesn’t even cover it. It’s been… incredible. Amazing.  

  

He stops walking, turning to face her fully.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

I mean, Sherry, I’m having the time of my life right now.  

  

Sherry blinks, her cheeks flushing slightly at his intensity.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s a big statement.  

  

Jeff laughs, running a hand through his hair.  

  

**JEFF**  

It is, but it’s true.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Confessions**  

  

He starts pacing slightly, his words tumbling out in rapid succession.  

  

**JEFF**  

The last six weeks—hell, the last few days—have been full of joy and wonder. I don’t think I’ve ever felt this… comfortable.  

  

Sherry watches him, her expression softening as he continues.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

You make it so easy for me to just… be myself. Not the rock star. Not the guy everyone thinks I’m supposed to be. Just me.  

  

He stops, turning back to her with a wide grin.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

And the sex? Sherry, it’s the best I’ve ever had. Hands down.  

  

Sherry laughs, covering her face briefly with her hand.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay, that’s… blunt.  

  

Jeff shrugs, his grin unapologetic.  

  

**JEFF**  

What can I say? I’m honest.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Thoughts on Family**  

  

He steps closer, his tone growing more thoughtful.  

  

**JEFF**  

You know, I think Jeremy would like you.  

  

Sherry raises an eyebrow, intrigued.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Your brother?  

  

Jeff nods, his hands gesturing animatedly as he speaks.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. But not in that way. I mean, he’d like you as *my* girlfriend, not someone he’d… you know.  

  

Sherry laughs, shaking her head.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Good to know.  

  

Jeff chuckles, his grin softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Seriously, though. He’s always been protective of me. I think he’d see how happy you make me.  

  

His gaze drifts back to the river, his voice quieter now.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

And maybe soon, you could meet my daughters.  

  

Sherry freezes slightly, her eyes widening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Your daughters?  

  

Jeff nods, glancing back at her.  

  

**JEFF**  

Yeah. I mean, not right away. But I think they’d love you.  

  

---

  

**The Flood of Emotions**  

  

Jeff steps forward again, his tone picking up speed.  

  

**JEFF**  

I just—I feel like this dam’s been building up inside me for years, and now it’s finally bursting.  

  

He gestures broadly, his voice brimming with emotion.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

You make me feel so alive, Sherry. Like I can breathe again. Like everything’s… better.  

  

Sherry stares at him, her chest tightening at the rawness of his words.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff…  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Response**  

  

Jeff pauses, his hands dropping to his sides as he studies her face.  

  

**JEFF**  

Too much?  

  

Sherry shakes her head quickly, stepping closer.  

  

**SHERRY**  

No. It’s… a lot, but it’s not too much.  

  

She places a hand on his arm, her voice softening.  

  

**SHERRY (CONT’D)**  

Thank you for telling me all of that.  

  

Jeff exhales, his shoulders relaxing slightly.  

  

**JEFF**  

I guess I needed to say it.  

  

Sherry nods, her lips curving into a faint smile.  

  

**SHERRY**  

And I needed to hear it.  

  

Jeff smiles back, his voice quieter now.  

  

**JEFF**  

Good.  

  

---

### **Scene 51: Sherry’s Silent Struggle**  

**Setting**: Little Miami River gorge, mid-afternoon. Jeff’s emotional confession overwhelms Sherry, triggering a visceral response deep within her psyche. The audience sees her internal battle play out in a flash of memories and emotions before she reclaims control, choosing to stay. This moment hinges entirely on Kate Mara’s ability to convey Sherry’s turmoil and resolution through subtle but powerful expressions.

  

---

  

**EXT. LITTLE MIAMI RIVER GORGE – MID-AFTERNOON**  

  

The serene landscape provides a stark contrast to the storm brewing within Sherry. Jeff stands before her, his wide grin softening as he senses her hesitation.  

  

**JEFF**  

(quietly)  

Sherry?  

  

The camera zooms in on Sherry’s face. Her expression tightens, her eyes darting to the frozen river as if searching for an escape route.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Flashbacks**  

  

The screen shifts to a rapid montage of Sherry’s past:  

  

- **Flashback 1**: A barely-legal Sherry in a white lace dress, standing beside a nervous young man in a courthouse wedding. Her parents look on disapprovingly. The scene fades into a cramped, messy apartment filled with tension as teenage arguments boil over.  

  

- **Flashback 2**: A slightly older Sherry, laughing and twirling with her second husband, a charismatic man with a scruffy beard. The montage cuts abruptly to their cluttered kitchen, stacks of unpaid bills on the counter, and Sherry’s devastated face as he walks out the door with a duffel bag.  

  

- **Flashback 3**: Sherry sitting in a lawyer’s office, signing divorce papers with trembling hands, a single tear rolling down her cheek.  

  

The screen flashes back to Sherry in the present, her breathing shallow and her chest rising and falling rapidly.  

  

---

  

**Physical Reaction**  

  

Sherry’s hand rises briefly to her temple, her fingers trembling. The camera lingers on her face, capturing the flash of fear, frustration, and exhaustion. Her eyes close tightly for a beat.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Not again. Not this time.  

  

She exhales sharply, her lips parting slightly as her gaze shifts back to Jeff. Her jaw tightens, and her eyes search his face for sincerity.  

  

---

  

**The Decision**  

  

The camera captures the transformation in real-time.  

  

- **First Beat**: Sherry’s brows furrow, her eyes narrowing slightly as doubt and self-preservation grip her.  

- **Second Beat**: Her gaze softens, her lips pressing together as her higher reasoning takes over.  

- **Third Beat**: A faint, almost imperceptible nod of her head. Her shoulders relax, and a flicker of a smile touches her lips.  

  

Jeff’s face brightens slightly, unaware of the turmoil she has just conquered.  

  

---

  

**Silent Connection**  

  

The camera holds on Sherry’s face for three long seconds. Her eyes shine with a mix of vulnerability and determination. She reaches out, taking Jeff’s hand in hers, her grip firm.  

  

Jeff’s smile widens, and he squeezes her hand gently.  

  

**JEFF**  

You okay?  

  

Sherry nods, her voice calm but steady.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah.  

  

---

  

**Camera Shots and Sound Editing**  

  

**Camera Shots**:  

- Tight close-ups of Sherry’s face, capturing every flicker of emotion as she processes her past and present.  

- Quick, jarring cuts to the flashbacks, with a washed-out filter to differentiate them from the present.  

- A lingering shot of Jeff’s hopeful expression, grounding Sherry in the moment.  

  

**Sound Editing**:  

- The wind rustling through the trees fades into a faint, rhythmic thrum mimicking Sherry’s heightened pulse during the flashbacks.  

- The sound abruptly shifts to stillness as Sherry regains control, the quiet broken only by her steadying breath.  

  

---

### **Scene 52: An External Event Tests Sherry’s Resolve**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s home, early evening. The cozy living room is softly lit, the sound of clicks and keyboard taps filling the space as Sherry plays an online game. The peaceful moment is shattered by an unexpected event that challenges her trust in Jeff and tests her emotional resolve.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – EVENING**  

  

Sherry sits on the couch, her laptop perched on her knees. The glow from the screen illuminates her face as she leans forward, engrossed in her game. She’s wearing a comfortable sweatshirt and leggings, her hair loosely tied back.  

  

The faint hum of the furnace and the occasional click of the mouse add to the tranquil atmosphere.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(muttering)  

Come on… just one more level.  

  

Her lips curl into a satisfied smile as her in-game character achieves a victory. She pumps her fist triumphantly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yes!  

  

Her phone buzzes on the coffee table. Sherry glances at it, her smile fading slightly when she sees an unknown number. She hesitates before picking it up and answering.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Hello?  

  

---

  

**The Bombshell Call**  

  

The voice on the other end is low and hesitant.  

  

**VOICE (O.S.)**  

Is this Sherry?  

  

Sherry frowns, adjusting her position.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yes. Who’s this?  

  

The voice grows firmer, with an edge of irritation.  

  

**VOICE (O.S.)**  

I’m sorry to call you like this, but… I think we need to talk.  

  

Sherry’s grip on the phone tightens.  

  

**SHERRY**  

About what?  

  

There’s a pause, and then the voice continues.  

  

**VOICE (O.S.)**  

About Jeff.  

  

Sherry’s heart skips a beat, her posture stiffening.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Who are you?  

  

**VOICE (O.S.)**  

That doesn’t matter. What matters is that you’re not the only one.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Shock and Doubt**  

  

Sherry stands abruptly, pacing the room as her mind races.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Excuse me?  

  

The voice takes on a bitter tone.  

  

**VOICE (O.S.)**  

I’ve been seeing him too. For months. I thought you should know.  

  

Sherry’s breathing quickens, her free hand running through her hair.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I… I don’t believe you.  

  

The voice scoffs.  

  

**VOICE (O.S.)**  

Believe what you want. Just don’t say I didn’t warn you.  

  

The call ends abruptly, leaving Sherry staring at the phone, her mind swirling with doubt and anger.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Reaction**  

  

Sherry sinks onto the couch, her hand shaking slightly as she sets the phone down. Her gaze fixes on the laptop screen, but the bright colors of the game feel jarring now.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Not the only one?  

  

Her jaw tightens, and she exhales sharply, forcing herself to focus.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

It could be a lie. Someone trying to mess with me.  

  

Her gaze shifts to a framed photo of her and Jeff on the coffee table, their smiles radiant and carefree.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But what if it’s not?  

  

---

  

**Testing Her Resolve**  

  

Sherry stands again, pacing the room as conflicting emotions churn within her.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

We’ve been so good. So solid.  

  

Her mind flashes back to moments with Jeff: his laughter, his confessions, the way he looks at her like she’s the only person in the world.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Would he? Could he?  

  

She stops abruptly, gripping the back of the couch.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(out loud)  

No. He wouldn’t.  

  

Her voice falters slightly, and she shakes her head, trying to steady herself.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

I need to hear it from him.  

  

---

  

**Building Suspense**  

  

Sherry picks up her phone again, her thumb hovering over Jeff’s name in her contacts. The room feels unbearably quiet, the weight of the moment pressing down on her.  

  

The camera lingers on her face, capturing the flicker of doubt and determination in her expression. Finally, she presses the call button, raising the phone to her ear.  

  

The screen fades to black as the phone rings, leaving the audience in suspense.  

  

---

### **Scene 53: Jeff’s Perspective on the Call**  

**Setting**: Jeff is in a recording studio in Los Angeles, working with his bandmates on tracks for their upcoming album. The mood is light and creative until his phone buzzes, pulling him into a moment of tension and confusion. Sherry’s call blindsides him, and he struggles to process her tone and the implications of her questions.  

  

---

  

**INT. RECORDING STUDIO – EVENING**  

  

The studio is a mix of sleek, high-tech equipment and creative chaos—guitars leaned against the wall, scattered coffee cups, and lyric sheets strewn across the console. Jeff sits on a stool, strumming an acoustic guitar while Kathy listens intently.  

  

**JEFF**  

(playing a riff)  

What about this? Too upbeat?  

  

Kathy tilts her head, considering.  

  

**KATHY**  

Depends on the lyrics. Upbeat works if we undercut it with something dark.  

  

Jeff smirks, nodding.  

  

**JEFF**  

Dark’s kind of our thing, isn’t it?  

  

Kathy laughs, leaning back in her chair.  

  

**KATHY**  

We’re not exactly sunshine and rainbows.  

  

---

  

**The Call Interrupts**  

  

Jeff’s phone buzzes on the console, lighting up with Sherry’s name. He glances at it, his expression softening.  

  

**JEFF**  

Hold on.  

  

He picks up the phone, stepping out of the studio into the hallway.  

  

---

  

**INT. STUDIO HALLWAY – CONTINUOUS**  

  

Jeff leans against the wall, his tone light as he answers.  

  

**JEFF**  

Hey, beautiful. What’s up?  

  

There’s a pause on the other end, and Jeff’s brow furrows slightly.  

  

**JEFF**  

Sherry?  

  

Her voice comes through, tight and hesitant.  

  

**SHERRY (O.S.)**  

Hey.  

  

Jeff straightens, sensing the tension.  

  

**JEFF**  

Everything okay?  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Confusion**  

  

Sherry’s tone wavers, a mix of doubt and determination.  

  

**SHERRY (O.S.)**  

Can I ask you something?  

  

Jeff frowns, his free hand rubbing the back of his neck.  

  

**JEFF**  

Of course. What’s going on?  

  

**SHERRY (O.S.)**  

Have you… been seeing anyone else?  

  

Jeff’s eyes widen, his posture stiffening.  

  

**JEFF**  

What? No. Why would you even ask that?  

  

There’s another pause, and Jeff’s grip on the phone tightens.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

Sherry, where’s this coming from?  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Internal Reaction**  

  

The camera shifts to Jeff’s face as a wave of emotions crosses it—confusion, frustration, and hurt.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

Who put this in her head?  

  

He leans back against the wall, exhaling sharply.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

We’ve been good. Solid. Haven’t we?  

  

He glances back toward the studio, his mind racing.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

This can’t be coming from her. Someone’s stirring shit up.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Reassurance**  

  

Jeff softens his tone, trying to steady himself and calm Sherry.  

  

**JEFF**  

Sherry, listen to me. I don’t know who’s saying what, but it’s not true.  

  

**SHERRY (O.S.)**  

You’re sure?  

  

Jeff presses his palm against his forehead, his voice firm but gentle.  

  

**JEFF**  

I’m sure. There’s no one else. Just you.  

  

The line is silent for a beat, and Jeff closes his eyes briefly.  

  

**JEFF (CONT’D)**  

You believe me, right?  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Response and Jeff’s Doubt**  

  

Sherry’s voice softens slightly, but the tension remains.  

  

**SHERRY (O.S.)**  

I… I want to.  

  

Jeff exhales, his chest tightening.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

That’s not a yes.  

  

He straightens, glancing toward the studio door as muffled laughter filters through.  

  

**JEFF (V.O.)**  

This isn’t over. Not by a long shot.  

  

---

### **Scene 54: Sherry Processes Jeff’s Boneheaded Reply**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s living room, early evening. Sherry sits frozen on the couch after Jeff’s clumsy reassurance that he hasn’t slept with anyone else “for at least three months.” The poorly phrased comment sends her mind spiraling, forcing her to process his response and evaluate their relationship anew.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – EVENING**  

  

Sherry’s phone sits on speaker mode on the coffee table as Jeff’s voice filters through.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

I mean, I haven’t slept with anyone else… for at least three months.  

  

The words hang in the air like an errant firework that exploded too close to the ground. Sherry blinks, her expression slowly shifting from disbelief to irritation.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(quietly, to herself)  

At least three months?  

  

She picks up the phone, her voice calm but icy.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

Yeah?  

  

**SHERRY**  

Did you hear what you just said?  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Response**  

  

There’s a pause, and Jeff’s voice comes back, hesitant.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

I… didn’t mean it like that.  

  

Sherry exhales sharply, her fingers gripping the phone tighter.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Then how did you mean it?  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

I mean, it’s been just you for months. Longer than that.  

  

Sherry’s brow furrows, her voice growing more pointed.  

  

**SHERRY**  

You could’ve just said that.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

I know. I’m sorry. I didn’t think—  

  

Sherry cuts him off, her tone sharper now.  

  

**SHERRY**  

No kidding.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Internal Reaction**  

  

She sets the phone down, pressing her fingers to her temples as Jeff’s voice continues in the background.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

Sherry, you know how I feel about you. I’m just… not great with words sometimes.  

  

Sherry closes her eyes, inhaling deeply.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Not great with words? Try not great with basic human communication.  

  

She shakes her head, opening her eyes to stare at the photo of them on the coffee table.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s not lying. At least, I don’t think he is.  

  

Her gaze shifts to the corner of the room, unfocused as she tries to make sense of her emotions.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But what does “at least three months” even mean? That it could’ve been four? Five?  

  

Her chest tightens as a wave of doubt washes over her.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Or does it mean that three months ago, he wasn’t thinking about me at all?  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Struggle to Focus**  

  

Jeff’s voice grows fainter as Sherry’s thoughts drown him out.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Why does he have to make everything so complicated?  

  

She clenches her fists briefly before relaxing them, forcing herself to listen.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

Sherry? Are you still there?  

  

Sherry leans forward, resting her elbows on her knees and picking up the phone.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. I’m here.  

  

Jeff exhales audibly, relief evident in his tone.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

Look, I’m sorry. I screwed that up.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Push for Clarity**  

  

Sherry rubs her temple, her voice steadier now.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff, I need you to be honest with me. Completely honest.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

I am.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Okay, then. When was the last time you slept with someone else?  

  

There’s a pause, and Sherry’s grip on the phone tightens.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

It was… before we got serious.  

  

Sherry leans back, her expression guarded.  

  

**SHERRY**  

And when exactly did we get serious?  

  

Jeff hesitates again, his voice quieter now.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

I don’t know. It kind of snuck up on me.  

  

Sherry closes her eyes briefly, exhaling slowly.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff, that’s not an answer.  

  

---

  

**Processing the Response**  

  

Jeff sighs audibly, his tone apologetic.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

You’re right. It’s not. I just… I’m not used to this. To us.  

  

Sherry’s lips press into a thin line as she absorbs his words.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

He’s trying. But is that enough?  

  

Her gaze drifts back to the photo on the coffee table, her expression softening slightly.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

Do I want this enough to deal with the mess?  

  

She sets the phone back on the coffee table, her voice quieter now.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Jeff, we’ll talk about this later.  

  

---

  

**Jeff’s Response**  

  

Jeff’s voice is hesitant but understanding.  

  

**JEFF (O.S.)**  

Okay. Just… don’t shut me out, Sherry.  

  

Sherry’s chest tightens at his words, and she nods absently.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I won’t.  

  

She ends the call, the room falling into silence once more.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Final Reflection**  

  

Sherry leans back on the couch, staring at the ceiling.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

I want to believe him.  

  

Her gaze shifts to the photo again, her expression softening.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

But wanting to believe isn’t the same as knowing.  

  

She sighs deeply, running a hand through her hair.  

  

**SHERRY (V.O.)**  

This isn’t over.  

  

The camera lingers on her thoughtful expression as the screen fades to black.  

  

---

### **Scene 55: Sherry Spills Her Guts**  

**Setting**: Sherry’s living room, early evening. After her unsettling phone call with Jeff, Sherry dials her sister, needing to vent. The conversation quickly turns into an amusing yet revealing interrogation, with Sherry’s sister calling her out on her behavior and forcing her to confront her own actions.  

  

---

  

**INT. SHERRY’S LIVING ROOM – EVENING**  

  

Sherry paces the room, her phone pressed to her ear. She’s still wearing her cozy sweatshirt and leggings, but her expression is frazzled, and her movements are restless.  

  

**SHERRY**  

(pacing)  

I need to talk.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

(sighs)  

Of course you do.  

  

**SHERRY**  

It’s Jeff.  

  

Her sister’s tone immediately grows sharper.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

What did he do now?  

  

**SHERRY**  

He said—ugh, it doesn’t even matter how he said it. He basically implied that it’s been “at least three months” since he’s been with anyone else.  

  

---

  

**The Sister’s Reaction**  

  

There’s a beat of silence before her sister bursts out laughing.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

“At least three months”? Oh, Sherry, come on!  

  

Sherry stops pacing, her face flushing.  

  

**SHERRY**  

I know! It’s ridiculous, right?  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Ridiculous doesn’t even begin to cover it. But let’s be real here, sis. How many men have *you* been with since the divorce?  

  

Sherry’s eyes widen, and she sputters.  

  

**SHERRY**  

What? Why does that even matter?  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

It matters because you’re over here grilling him, and I’m just wondering if you’re living in a glass house.  

  

---

  

**Sherry’s Deflection**  

  

Sherry plops onto the couch, crossing her legs defensively.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s different.  

  

Her sister’s tone turns wry.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Oh, is it? Enlighten me.  

  

Sherry fidgets with the hem of her sweatshirt, her voice quieter now.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Look, Jeff’s a rock star. His life is… bigger. Messier.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Uh-huh. And your life’s been a picture of restraint?  

  

Sherry groans, covering her face with her hand.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Why do you always do this?  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Because you call me every time you’re in a mess, Sherry. Now spill.  

  

---

  

**Sherry Starts Spilling**  

  

Sherry sighs heavily, leaning back against the couch.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Fine. Since the divorce… there was Todd.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

The personal trainer?  

  

**SHERRY**  

Yeah. And then there was Brad…  

  

Her sister interrupts, her tone incredulous.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Wait, Brad the IT guy? The one who couldn’t stop talking about Bitcoin?  

  

Sherry groans, her head falling back against the couch.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Don’t remind me.  

  

Her sister laughs, the sound both exasperated and amused.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Okay, so that’s two. Who else?  

  

Sherry hesitates, her voice quieter.  

  

**SHERRY**  

There was Peter… and—  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

(quickly)  

Peter the *married* guy?  

  

Sherry winces.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Technically, he was separated.  

  

Her sister lets out a long, dramatic sigh.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Sherry, you’re exhausting.  

  

---

  

**The Big Question**  

  

Sherry sits up straighter, her tone defensive.  

  

**SHERRY**  

Why does any of this matter?  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Because you’re acting like Jeff’s the only one bringing baggage to this relationship.  

  

Sherry’s face flushes, and she stares at the floor.  

  

**SHERRY**  

That’s not fair.  

  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Isn’t it? You’ve got a thing for men who complicate your life, Sherry. Todd, Brad, Peter… now Jeff.  

  

Sherry’s lips press into a thin line as her sister’s words hit home.  

  

**SHERRY**  

This is different.  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

OK. How?  

---

**Sherry Explains Herself**  
  
Sherry takes a deep breath, her voice softer now.  

**SHERRY**  

Because with Jeff… I feel seen. Like I’m not just someone he’s passing time with.  

Her sister’s tone softens slightly.  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

And you’re sure he feels the same?  

Sherry hesitates, her gaze drifting to the photo of her and Jeff on the coffee table.  

**SHERRY**  

I think so.  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Then talk to him, Sherry. Really talk to him. Because if you keep calling me instead of dealing with your own issues, you’re going to mess this up.  

---

**Sherry’s Resolve**  

Sherry exhales, a small smile tugging at her lips despite herself.  

**SHERRY**  

You’re annoyingly good at this, you know that?  

Her sister laughs softly.  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

That’s what I’m here for.  

Sherry glances at the phone, her voice more determined now.  

**SHERRY**  

Thanks, sis.  

**SISTER (O.S.)**  

Anytime. Just… maybe not at 7 AM next time, okay?  

Sherry laughs, shaking her head as the call ends.  

---
